Tad anuttaraɱ Brahma-cariya-pariyosānaɱ diṭṭhe'va dhamme sayaɱ abhiññā sacchi-katvā upasampajja vihāsi. Khiṇā jāti vusitaɱ Brahma-cariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇiɱ nāparaɱ itthāntāyāti abbhaññāsi aññataro ca kho pan'āyasmā Bhāradvājo Arahattaɱ ahositi.|| ||

Sundarika-Bhāradvāja Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

5. Māgha Suttaɱ

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Gijjhaguṭe pabbate. Atha kho Māgho māṇavo yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi, sammodaniyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇiyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi. Eka-m-antaɱ nisanno kho Māgho māṇavo [87] Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: || ||

Ahaɱ hi bho Gotama, dāyako dāna-pati vadaññu yā cayogo, dhammena bhoge pariyesāmi, dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhamma-laddhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekasasā pi dadāmi, davinnam pi dadāmi, tiṇṇam pi dadāmi, catunnam pi dadāmi, pañcannam pi dadāmi, chattam pi dadāmi, sattannam pi dadāmi, aṭṭhannam pi dadāmi, vanannam pi dadāmi, dasannam pi dadāmi, visāya pi dadāmi, tiɱsāya pi dadāmi, cattārisāya pi dadāmi, paññāsāya pi dadāmi, satassa pi dadāmi, bhiyyo pi dadāmi. Kacc'āhaɱ bho Gotamaɱ evaɱ dadanto evaɱ yajanto bahuɱ puññaɱ pasavāmi" ti. "Tagagha tvaɱ māṇava, evaɱ dadanto evaɱ yajanto bahuɱ puññaɱ pasavāsi, yo kho māṇava dāyako dāna-pati vadaññū yā cayogo dhammena bhoge pariyesati dhammena bhoge pariyesitvā dhamma-laddhehi bhogehi dhammādhigatehi ekasasā pi dadāmi, davinnam pi dadāmi, tiṇṇam pi dadāmi, catunnam pi dadāmi, pañcannam pi dadāmi, chattam pi dadāmi, sattannam pi dadāmi, aṭṭhannam pi dadāmi, vanannam pi dadāmi, dasannam pi dadāmi, visāya pi dadāmi, tiɱsāya pi dadāmi, cattārisāya pi dadāmi, paññāsāya pi dadāmi, satassa pi dadāmi, bhiyyo pi dadāmi.|| ||

Kacc'āhaɱ bho Gotamaɱ ekaɱ dadanto evaɱ yajanto bahuɱ puññaɱ pasavāmiti.|| ||

Atha kho Māgho māṇavo Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi.|| ||

487. "Pucchām'abhaɱ bho Gotamaɱ vadaññuɱ (iti Māgho māṇavo)||
Kāsāyavāsiɱ agihaɱ carantaɱ||
Yo yā cayogo dāna-pati gahaṭṭo,||
puññatthiko yajati puññapekho||
[88] Dadaɱ paresaɱ idha annapānaɱ||
Kattha hutaɱ yajamānassa sujjhe."|| ||

488. "Yo yā cayogo dāna-pati gahaṭṭho (Māghā ti Bhagavā)||
Puññatthiko yajati puññapekho||
Dadaɱ paresaɱ idha annapānaɱ||
Ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyye hi tādi."|| ||

489. "Yo yā cayogo dāna-pati gahaṭṭho (iti Māgho māṇavo)||
Puññatthiko yajati puññapekho||
Dadaɱ paresaɱ idha annapānaɱ,||
Akkhāhi me Bhagavā dakkhiṇeyye."|| ||

490. "Yo ve asattā vicaranti loke||
Akiñcanā kevalino yatattā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche,||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

491. Ye sabbasaŋyojanabandhanacchidā||
Dantā vimutatā anīghā nirāsā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche,||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

492. Ye sabbasaŋyojanavippamuttā||
Dantā vimuttā anīghā nirāsā||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

493. Rāgañ ca dosañ ca pahāya mohaɱ||
Khiṇāsavā vusitabrahma-cariyā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

494. Yesu na māyā vasati na māno,||
[89] Ye vitalobhā amamā nirasā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

495. Ye ve na taṇhāsu upātipannā||
Vitareyya oghaɱ amamā caranti,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

496. Yesaɱ taṇhā n'atthi kuhiñci loke||
Bhavābhavāya idha vā huraɱ vā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

497. Ye kāme hitvā agihā caranti||
Susaññatattā tasaraɱva ujjuɱ||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

498. Ye vitarāgā susamābhitindriyā||
Cando va Rāhu-gahaṇā pamuttā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

499 Samitāvino vitarāgā akopā||
Yesaɱ gati n'atthi idha vippahāya,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

500. Jahitvā jāti-maraṇaɱ asesaɱ||
Kathaɱ-kathaɱ sabbam upātivattā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

501. Ye attadipā vicaranti loke||
Akiñcanā sabbadhi vippamuttā,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

502. Ye h'ettha jānanti yathā tathā idaɱ||
'Ayam antimā, n'atthi puna-b-bhavo' ti,||
Kālena tesaɱ havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha.|| ||

[90] 503. Yo vedagu jhānarato satimā||
Sambodhipatto saraṇaɱ bahunnaɱ,||
Kālena tamhi havyaɱ pavecche||
Yo brāhmaṇo puññapekho yajetha."|| ||

504. "Addhā amoghā mama pucchānā ahu,||
Akkhāsi me Bhagavā dakkhiṇeyye,||
Tvaɱ h'ettha jānāsi yathā tathā idaɱ||
Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo.|| ||

505. Yo yā cayogo dāna-pati gahaṭṭho iti Māgho māṇavo||
Puññatthiko yajati puññapekho,||
Dadaɱ paresaɱ idha annapānaɱ||
Akkhāhi me Bhagavā yañña-sampadaɱ."|| ||

506. "Yajassu yajamāno Māghā ti Bhagavā||
Sabbattha vippasādehi cittaɱ,||
Ārammaṇaɱ yajamānassa yaññaɱ,||
Ettha patiṭṭāya jahāti dosaɱ.|| ||

507. So vitarāgo pavineyya dosaɱ||
Mettaɱ citataɱ bhāvayaɱ appamāṇaɱ,||
Rattin-divaɱ satataɱ appamatto||
Sabbā disā pharate appamaññaɱ.|| ||

508. "Ko sujjhati muccati bhajjhati ca,||
Ken'attanā gacchati Brahma-lokaɱ,||
Ajānato me muni brūhi puṭṭho||
Bhagavā hi me sakkhi Brahm'ajja diṭṭho||
[91] Tuvaɱ hi no brahmasamo ti saccaɱ||
Kathaɱ uppajjati Brahma-lokaɱ jutimā."|| ||

509. "Yo yajati tividhaɱ yañña-sampadaɱ, (Māghā ti Bhagavā)||
Ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyyehi tadi,||
Evaɱ yajitvā sammā yā cayogo||
Upapajjati Brahma-lokan ti brūmi" ti.|| ||

Evaɱ vutte Māgho māṇavo Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Abhikkantaɱ bho goma seyyathā pibho Gotama, kikkujjitaɱ vā ukkujjeya, paṭi-c-channaɱ vā vivareyya, muḷhassavā Maggaɱ ācikkheyya, andha-kāre vā tela-pajjotaɱ dhāreyya cakkhu-manto rūpāni dakkhintiti, evam evaɱ bhotā Gotamena aneka-pariyāyena dhammo pakāsito, ete mayaɱ bhavantaɱ Gotamaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāma Dhammañ ca bhikkhu-Saŋghañca, upāsake no bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajja-t-agge pāṇupete saraṇaɱ gatanti.|| ||

Māgha Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

6. Sabhiya Suttaɱ

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane Kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena Sabhiyassa paribbājakassa purāṇasālohitāya devatāya pañhā udadiṭṭhā honti: "Yo te Sabhiya samano vā brāhmaṇo vā ime pañeha puṭṭho vyākaroti, tassa santike Brahma-cariyaɱ careyyāsi" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbajāko tassā devatāya santike te pañhe uggahetvā, ye te samaṇa-brāhmaṇā saŋghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā [92] sādhusammatā bahu-janassa, seyyath'idaɱ: Purāṇo Kassapo Makkhali Gosālo Ajito Kesakamabali Pakudho Kaccāyano Sañajayo Bellaṭṭhiputto Nigaṇṭho Nātaputto. Te upasankamitvā te pañeha pucchati. Te Sabhiyena paribbajakena pañeha puṭṭhā na sampāyanti. Asampāyantā kopañ ca dosañ ca appaccayañ ca pātu-karonti, api ca Sabhiyañ ñeva paribbājakaɱ paṭipucchanti. Atha kho Sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etad ahosi: 'ye kho te bhonto samaṇa-brāhmaṇā saŋghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahu-janassa, seyyath'īdaɱ: Purāṇo Kassapo Makkhali Gosālo Ajito Kesakamabali Pakudho Kaccāyano Sañajayo Bellaṭṭhiputto Nigaṇṭho Nātaputto. Te mayā pañeha puṭṭhā na sampāyanti asampāyanatā kopañ ca dosañ ca appaccayañ ca pātukāronti, api ca mamaññev'ettha paṭipucchanti: yan nunāhaɱ hināyāvattitvā kāme paribhuñejayyan' ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etad ahosi: 'ayam pi samaṇo Gotamo saŋghi c'eva gaṇi ca gaṇācariyo ca ñāto yasassi titthakaro sādhusammāto bahu-janassa: yan nunāhaɱ samaṇaɱ Gotamaɱ upasankamitvā ime pañeha puccheyyan' ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbajākassā etad ahosi: 'ye pi kho te bhanto samaṇa-brāhmaṇā jiṇaṇā vuddhā mahallakā addhagatā vayo anuppattā therā rattaññu cira-pabba-jitā saŋghino gaṇino gaṇācariyā ñātā yasassino titthakarā sādhusammatā bahu-janassa, seyyath'idaɱ: Purāṇo Kassapo [93] Makkhali Gosālo Ajito Kesakamabali Pakudho Kaccāyano Sañajayo Bellaṭṭhiputto Nigaṇṭho Nātaputto. Te pi mayā pañeha puṭṭho na sampāyanti. Asampāyantā kopañ ca dosañ ca appaccayañ ca pātu-karonti, api ca mañ ñev'ettha paṭipucchanti. Kaɱ pana me samaṇo Gotamo ime pañeha puṭṭho vyākarisasati, samaṇo hi Gotamo daharo c'eva jātiyā navo ca pabbajāyā' ti. Atha kho Sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etad ahosi: 'samaṇo kho "daharo" ti na uññātabbo na paribhotabbo, daharo pi ce samaṇo hoti, so ca hoti mahiddhiko mah-ā-nubhāvo, yan nunāhaɱ samaṇaɱ Gotamaɱ upasankamitvā ime pañeha puccheyyan' ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako yena Rājāgahaɱ tena cārikaɱ pakkāmi. Anupubbena cārikaɱ cara-māno yena Rājagahaɱ Veḷuvanaɱ Kalandakanivāpo, yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ samemādi, sammodaniyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇiyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi, eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Sabhiyo paribabājako Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhābhāsi:|| ||

510. "Kaŋkhi vecikicchi āgamaɱ (iti Sabhiyo)||
Pañeha pucchituɱ abhikaŋkhamāno,||
Tes'antakaro bhavāhi me,||
pañeha me puṭṭho anupubbaɱ anudhammaɱ vyākarohi me."|| ||

[94] 511. "Durato āgato si Sabhiyā (ti Bhagavā)||
Pañeha pucchituɱ abhikamkhamāno,||
Tes'antakaro bhavāhami te,||
pañeha te puṭṭho anupubbaɱ anudhammaɱ vyākarohi te.|| ||

512. Puccha maɱ Sabhiya pañhaɱ, yaɱ kiñci manas'icchasi,||
Tassa tass'eva pañahassa ahaɱ antaɱ karomi te" ti|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyassa paribbājakassa etad ahosi: "acchariyaɱ vata bho, abbhutaɱ vata bho, yaɱ vatāhaɱ aññesu samaṇa-brāhmaṇesu okāsamattam pi nālatthaɱ, taɱ me idaɱ samaṇena Gotamena okāsakammaɱ katan" ti atta-mano pamodito udaggo pitisomanassajāto Bhagavantaɱ pañhaɱ pucchi: || ||

513. "Kiɱ pattinam āhu bhikkhunaɱ (iti Sabhiyo)||
Sorataɱ kena, kathañ ca dannam āhu,||
Buddho ti kathaɱ pacuccati,||
Puṭṭho me Bhagavā vyākarohi."|| ||

[95] 514. "Pajjena katena antanā (Sabhiyā ti Bhagavā) pari-Nibbānagato vitiṇñakaŋkho,||
vibhavañ ca bhavañ ca vipa-p-pahāya||
Vusitavā khiṇapuna-b-bhavo sa bhikkhu.|| ||

515. Sabbattha upekkhako satimā||
Na so hiɱsati kañci sabba-loke,||
Tiṇṇo samaṇo anāvilo,||
Ussadā yassa na santi, sorato so.|| ||

516. Yass'indriyāni bhāvitāni||
Ajjhantaɱ bahiddhā ca sabba-loke,||
Nibbijjha imaɱ parañ ca lokaɱ||
Kālaɱ kankhati bhāvito, sa danto.|| ||

517. Kappāni viceyya kevalāni||
Saɱsāraɱ dubhayaɱ cut'upapātaɱ,||
Vigatarajam anaŋgaṇaɱ visuddhaɱ||
Pattaɱ jātikkhayaɱ tam āhu buddhan" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinan'ditvā anumo-ditvā atta-mano pamodito udaggo pitisomanassajāto Bhagavantaɱ uttariɱ pañahaɱ pucchi: || ||

518. "Kiɱ pattinamāhu brāhmaṇaɱ (iti Sabhiyo)||
Samaṇaɱ kena kathañ ca nhātako ti,||
[96] Nāgo ti kathaɱ pavuccati||
Puṭṭho me Bhagavā vyākarohi."|| ||

519. "Bāhitvā sabbapāpāni (Sabhiyāti Bhagavā)||
Vimalo sādhu samāhito ṭhitatto,||
Saɱsāram aticca kevali so,||
Asito tādi pavuccate (sa) brāhmā.|| ||

520. Samitāvi pahāya puññapāpaɱ||
Virajo ñatvā imaɱ parañ ca lokaɱ,||
Jātimaraṇaɱ upātivatto||
Samaṇo tādi pacuccate tathattā.|| ||

521. Ninhāya sabbapāpakāni||
Ajjhattaɱ bahiddhā ca sabba-loke,||
Dvemanussesu kappiyesu||
Kappaɱ n'eti tam āhu nhātako ti.|| ||

522. Āguɱ na karoti kiñci loke,||
Sabbasaɱyoge visajja bandhanāni;||
Sabbattha na sajjati vimutto||
Nāgo tadi pavuccate tathattā" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinan'ditvā anumo-ditvā atta-mano pamodito udaggo pitisomanassajāto Bhagavantaɱ uttariɱ pañahaɱ pucchi: || ||

523. "Kaɱ khettajinaɱ vadanti buddhā (iti Sabhiyo)||
Kusalaɱ kena kathañ ca paṇḍito ti,||
[97] Muni nāma kathaɱ pavuccati||
Puṭṭho me Bhagavā vyākarohi."|| ||

524. "Khettāni viveyya kevalāni (Sabhiyāti Bhagavā)||
Divyaɱ mānusakañ ca brahmakhettaɱ,||
Sabbakhettamūlabandhanā pamutto||
Khettajino tadi pavuccate tathattā.|| ||

525. Kosāni viceyya kevalāni||
Dibbaɱ mānusakañ ca brahmakosaɱ,||
Sabbakosamūlabandhanā pamutto||
Kusalo tādi pavuccate tathattā.|| ||

526. Dubhayāni viveyya paṇḍarāni||
Ajjhattaɱ bahiddhā ca sudadhipañño,||
Kaṇhaɱ-sukkam upātivatto||
Paṇḍito tādi pavuccate tathattā.|| ||

527. Asatañ ca satañ ca ñatvā dhammaɱ||
Ajjhattaɱ bahiddhā ca sabba-loke,||
Devamananussehi pujaniyo so||
Saŋgaɱ jālam aticca so muni" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinan'ditvā anumo-ditvā atta-mano pamodito udaggo pitisomanassajāto Bhagavantaɱ uttariɱ pañahaɱ pucchi: || ||

[98] 528. "Kiɱ pattinam āhu vedaguɱ (iti Sabhiyo)||
Anuviditaɱ kena, kathañ ca viriyavā ti,||
Ājāniyo kin ti nāma hoti,||
Puṭṭho me Bhagavā vyākarohi."|| ||

529. "Vedāni viceyya kevalāni (Sabhiyā ti Bhagavā)||
Samaṇānaɱ yāni p'atthi brāhmaṇānaɱ,||
Sabba vedanāsu vitarāgo||
Sabbaɱ vedam aticca vedagu so.|| ||

530. Anuvicca papañca nāma-rūpaɱ||
Ajjhattaɱ bahiddhā ca rogamulaɱ,||
Sabbarogamūlabandhanā pamutto||
Anuvidito tādi pavuccate tathattā|| ||

531. Virato idha sabbapāpakehi||
Nirayadukkham aticca viriyavā so,||
So viriyavā padhānavā||
Dhiro tādi pavuccate tathattā.|| ||

532. Yass'asasu lutāni bandhanāni||
Ajjhattaɱ bahiddhā ca saŋgamūlaɱ,||
Sabbasaŋgamūlabandhanā pamutto||
Ājāniyo tādi pavuccate tathattā" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinan'ditvā anumo-ditvā atta-mano pamodito udaggo pitisomanassajāto Bhagavantaɱ uttariɱ pañahaɱ pucchi: || ||

533. "Kiɱ panttinam āhu sottiyaɱ (iti Sabhiyo)||
[99] Ariyaɱ kena, kathañ ca caraṇavā ti,||
Paribbājako kin ti nāma hoti||
Puṭṭho me Bhagavā vyākarohi."|| ||

534. "Sutvā sabba-dhammaɱ abhiññāya loke (Sabhiyā ti Bhagavā)||
Sāvajjānavajjaɱ yad atthi kiñci,||
Abhibhuɱ akathaɱ-kathiɱ vimuttaɱ||
Anighaɱ sabbadhi-m-āhu sottiyo" ti.|| ||

535. Chetvā āsavāni ālayāni||
Vidvā so na upeti gabbhaseyyaɱ,||
Saññaɱ tividhaɱ panujja paŋkaɱ||
Kappan n'eti tam āhu ariyo ti.|| ||

536. Yo idha caraṇesu pantipatto||
Kusalo sabbadā ājāni dhammaɱ,||
Sabbattha na sajjati vimutto||
Paṭighā yass na santi, caraṇavā so.|| ||

537. Dukkhavepakkaɱ yad atthi kammaɱ||
Uddham adho tiriyañ cāpi majjhe,||
Paribbājayitā pariññacāri||
Māyaɱ mānam atho pi lobhako'dhaɱ||
Pariyantam akāsi nāma-rūpaɱ||
Taɱ paribbājakam āhu pattipattan" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinan'ditvā anumo-ditvā atta-mano pamodito udaggo [100] pitisomanassajāto uṭṭhāy āsanā ekaɱsaɱ uttarā-saŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten'añajalim pāṇāmetvā Bhagavantaɱ samamukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi: || ||

538. "Yāni ca tīṇi yāni ca saṭṭhi||
Samaṇappavāda sitāni bhuripañña,||
Saññakkhara-saññanissitāni||
Osaraṇāni vineyya oghantam agā.|| ||

539. Antagu si pāragu dukkhassa,||
Arahāsi sammāSamBuddho, khiṇāsavaɱ taɱ maññe,||
Jutimā mutimā pahutapañño,||
Dukkhass'antakara atāresi maɱ.|| ||

540. Yaɱ me kaɱkhitam aññāsi||
Vicikicchāɱ maɱ atāresi, namo te,||
Muni monapathesu pattipatta||
Akhila Ādiccabandhu sorato si.|| ||

[101] 541. Yā me kaŋkhā pure āsi, taɱ me vyākāsi cakkhumā,||
Addhā muni si SamBuddho, n'atthi nivaraṇā tava.|| ||

542. Upāyāsā ca te sabbe viddhastā vinaḷīkatā,||
Sitibhūto damappatto dhitimā saccanikkamo.|| ||

543. Tassa te nāga nāgassa mahāvīrassa bhāsato,||
Sabbe devā anumodanti ubho Nārada-Pabbatā.|| ||

544. Namo te purisājañña, nāmo te puri Suttama,||
Sadevakasmiɱ lokasmiɱ n'atthi te paṭipuggalo.|| ||

545. Tuvaɱ Buddho tuvaɱ Satthā tuvaɱ Mārābhibhu muni,||
Tuvaɱ anusaye chetvā tiṇeṇā tāres'imaɱ pajaɱ.|| ||

546. Upadhi te samatikkantā, āsavā te padāḷitā,||
Siho si anupādāno pabhinabhayabheravo.|| ||

547. Puṇḍarikaɱ yathā vaggu toye na upalippati,||
Evaɱ puññe ca pāpe ca ubhaye tvaɱ na lippasi,||
Pāde vīra pasārehi, Sabhiyo vandati Satthuno" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama, abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama, seyyathā pi bho Gotama nikkujjitaɱ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭi-c-channaɱ vā vivareyya, muḷhassa vā Maggaɱ ācikkekhayya, andha-kāre vā tela pajjotaɱ dhareyya cakkhu-manto rūpāni dakkhinti, evam evaɱ bhotā Gotamena anekapariyāyevana dhammo pakāsito es'āhaɱ bhavantaɱ gomaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāmi Dhammañ ca bhikkhu Saŋghañca labheyyāhaɱ bhāneta, Bhagavato santike pabbajjaɱ labheyyaɱ [102] upasampadan" ti. "Yo kho Sabhiya, añña-titthiyapubbo imasmiɱ Dhamma-Vinaye ākankhati pabbajaɱ ākankhati upasampadaɱ, so cattāro māse parivasati, catunnaɱ māsānaɱ accayena āraddha-cittā bhikkhu pabbā-jenti upasampādenti bhikkhu bhāvāya, apica mettha puggalavemattatā viditā" ti.|| ||

"Sace bhante, añña-titthiya-pubbā imasmiɱ Dhamma-Vinaye ākaŋkhantā pabbajajaɱ ākaŋkhantā upasampadaɱ catutāro māse parivasanti, catunnaɱ māsānaɱ accayena āraddha-cittā bhikkhu pabbājenatti upasampādenti bhikkhu-bhāvāya, ahaɱ cattāri vassāni parivasissāmi, catunnaɱ vassānaɱ accayena āradadhacittā bhikkhu pabbājentu upasampādentu bhikkhu-bhāvāyāti. Alattha kho Sabhiyo paribbājako Bhagavato santake pabbajjaɱ alattha upasampadaɱ, dacir'ūpasampanno kho pan'āyasmā Bhāradvājo eko cupakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpi pahit'atto viharatto na cirasse ca yass'atthāya kula-puttā samma-d-eva agārasmā anagāriyaɱ pabbajanti.|| ||

Tad anuttaraɱ Brahma-cariya-pariyosānaɱ diṭṭhe'va dhamme sayaɱ abhiññā sacchi-katvā upasampajja vihāsi. Khiṇā jāti vusitaɱ Brahma-cariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇiɱ nāparaɱ itthāntāyāti abbhaññāsi aññataro ca kho pan'āyasmā Sabhiyo Arahattaɱ ahositi.|| ||

Sabhiya Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

7. Sela Suttaɱ

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Aŋguttarāpesu cārikaɱ cara-māno mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ aḍḍhateḷa- [103] sehi bhikkhu-satehi yena Āpaṇaɱ nāma Aŋguttarāpānaɱ nigamo tad avasari. Assosi kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo: "Samaṇo khalu bho Gotamo Sakya-putto Sakya-kulā pabba-jito Aŋguttarāpesu cārikaɱ cara-māno mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhu-satehi Āpaṇaɱ anuppatto, taɱ kho pana bhavantaɱ Gotamaɱ evaɱ kalyāṇo kitti-saddo abbhu-g-gato, "iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāSamBuddho vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno Sugato loka-vidu anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathi Satthā deva-manussānaɱ Buddho Bhagavā" ti so imaɱ lokaɱ sa-devakaɱ sa-mārakaɱ sabrahamakaɱ sa-s-samaṇa-brāhmaṇiɱ pajaɱ sadevamunassaɱ sayaɱ abhiññā sacchi-katvā pavedeti, so dhammaɱ deseti ādi-kalyāṇa majjhe kalyāṇaɱ pariyosāna-kalyāṇaɱ sātthaɱ savyañajanaɱ kevala-paripuṇaṇaɱ pariyuddhaɱ Brahma-cariyaɱ pakāseti, sādhu kho pana tathā-rūpānaɱ arahataɱ dasasnaɱ hoti" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi, sammodiniyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇiyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Keṇiyaɱ jaṭilaɱ Bhagavā dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaɱsesi.|| ||

Atha kho Keṇiyā jaṭilo Bhagavatā dhammiyā kathāya sanda-s-sito samāda-pito samutte-jito sampahaɱ-sito Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Adhivāsetu me bhavaɱ Gotamo svātanāya bhattaɱ saddhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghenā" ti, evaɱ vutto Bhagavā Keṇiyaɱ jaṭilaɱ etad avoca: "Mahā kho Keṇiya, [104] bhikkhu-saŋgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhu-satāni, tvañ ca kho brāhmaṇesu abhi-p-pasanno" ti. Dutiyam pi kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kiñ cāpi bho Gotama, mahā bhikkhasaŋgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhu-satāni, ahañ ca brāhmaṇesu abhi-p-pasanno, adhivāsetu me bhavaɱ Gotamo svātanāya bhattaɱ saddhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghenā" ti. Dutiyam pi kho Bhagavā Keṇiyo jaṭilaɱ etad avoca: "Mahā Keṇiya, bhikkhasaŋgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhu-satāni, tvañ ca kho brāhmaṇesu abhi-p-pasanno"ti. Tatiyam pi kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kiñ cāpi bho Gotama, mahā bhikkhasaŋgho aḍḍhateḷasāni bhikkhu-satāni, ahañ ca brāhmaṇesu abhi-p-pasanno, adhivāsetv-eva me bhavaɱ Gotamo svātanāya bhattaɱ saddhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghenā" ti.|| ||

Adhivāsesi Bhagavā tuṇahibhāvena.|| ||

Atha kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo Bhagavantaɱ adhivāsanaɱ viditvā uṭṭhāyasā yena sako assame ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā mitt-ā-macce ñātisālohite āmantesi: "Suṇantu me bhonto mittāmacacā ñātisā-lohitā samaṇo me Gotamo nimantito svātanāya bhattaɱ sadadhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghena yena me kāyaveyyāvaṭikaɱ kareyyā" ti.|| ||

"Evaɱ bho" ti kho Keṇiyassa jaṭilassa mitt-ā-maccā ñātisā-lohitā Keṇiyassa jaṭilassa paṭissutvā app-ekacce uddhanānani khaṇanti, app-ekacce kaṭṭhāni phālenti, app-ekacce bhājanti dhovanti, app-ekacce udaka-maṇikaɱ patiṭṭhāpenti, app-ekacce āsanāni paññā-penti. Keṇiyo pana jaṭilo sāmaɱ yeva maṇḍalamālaɱ paṭiyādeti.|| ||

Tena kho pana samayena Selo brāhmaṇo Āpaṇe paṭivasati [105] tiṇaṇaɱ vedānaɱ pāragu sanighaṇaṭukeṭubhānaɱ sākkhara-p-pabhe-dānaɱ itihāsa-pañca-mānaɱ padako veyyā-karaṇo lokāyatamahā-purisa-lakkhaṇesu anavayo, tīṇi māṇavakasatāni matte vāceti. Tena kho pana samayena Keṇiye jaṭile Sele brāhmaṇe abhi-p-pasanno hoti|| ||

Atha kho Selo brāhmaṇo tihi māṇavakasatehi parivuto jaŋghā-vihāraɱ anucaŋkammāno anuvicara-māno yena Keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo ten'upasankami. Addasā kho Selo brāhmaṇo Keṇiyasmiɱ jaṭile app-ekacce uddhanānani khaṇante, app-ekacce kaṭṭhāni phālenti, app-ekacce bhājanti dhovanti, app-ekacce udaka-maṇikaɱ patiṭṭhāpenti, app-ekacce āsanāni paññā-penti. Keṇiyaɱ pana jaṭilaɱ sāmañ ñeva maṇḍalamālaɱ paṭiyādentaɱ disvā Keṇiyaɱ jaṭilaɱ etad avoca: || ||

"Ki nu bhoto Keṇiyassa āvāho vā bhavissati, vihāho vā bhavissati, mahāyañño vā pacucapaṭṭhito, rājā vā Māgadho Seniyo Bimbisāro nimantino svātanāya saddhiɱ balakāyenā" ti?|| ||

"Na me Sela, āvāho bhavissati, na pi vihābho bhavissati, na pi rājā Māgadho Seniyeba Bimbisāro nimattito svātanāya saddhiɱ balakāyena, api ca kho me mahāyañño pacc'upaṭṭhito atithi. Samaṇo Gotamo Sakya-putto Sakya-kulā pabba-jito Aŋguttarāpesu cārikaɱ cara-māno mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ aḍḍhateḷasehi bhikkhu-satehi Āpaṇaɱ anuppatto. Taɱ kho [106] pana bhavantaɱ Gotamaɱ evaɱ kalyāṇo nitti saddo abbhu-g-gato "Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāSamBuddho vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno Sugato loka-vidu anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathi Satthā deva-manussānaɱ Buddho Bhagavā" ti so me nimattito svātanāya saddhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghenā" ti.|| ||

"Buddho" ti kho bho Keṇiya, vadesi? "'Buddho' ti bho Sela, vadāmi." "Buddho" ti bho Keṇiya, vadesi? "'Buddho' ti bho sela vadāmi" ti.|| ||

Atha bho Selassa brahmaṇassa etad ahosi: "Ghoso pi kho eso dullabho lokasmiɱ yadidaɱ 'Buddho' ti. Āgatāni kho pana asmākaɱ mantesu dvattiɱsa mahā-purisa-lakkhanāni, yehi samannāgatassa mahāpurisassa dve va gatiyo bhavanti anaññā. Sace agāraɱ ajjhāvasati, rājā hoti cakka-vatti dhammiko Dhamma-rājā cāturanto vijitāvi jana-padatthācariya-p-patto santaratanasamannāgato. Tass'imāni satta ratanāni bhavanti, seyyath'īdaɱ: cakka-ratanaɱ hatthi-ratanaɱ assa-ratanaɱ maṇi-ratanaɱ itthi-ratanaɱ gahapati-ratanaɱ pariṇāyakaratanam eva sattamaɱ, parosahassaɱ kho pan'assa puttā bhavatti surā viraŋgarūpā parasena-p-pamaddanā, so imaɱ paṭhaviɱ sāgarapariyantaɱ adaṇḍena asatthena dhammena abhivijiya ajjhāvasati. Sace kho panāgārasmā anagāriyaɱ pabbajati, arahaɱ hoti sammāSamBuddho loka vivatta-c-chaddo' —|| ||

"Kahaɱ pana bho Keṇiya, etarahi so bhavaɱ Gotamo viharati arahaɱ sammāsammuddho" ti?|| ||

Evaɱ vutte Keṇiyo jaṭilo dakkhiṇaɱ bāhaɱ paggahetvā Selaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ etad avoca: [107] "yen'esā bho Sela nilavanarāji" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Selo brāhmaṇo tihi māṇavakasatehi saddhiɱ yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkakami. Atha kho Selo brāhmaṇo te māṇavake āmantesi: "Appa-saddā honto āga-c-chantu pāde padaɱ nikkhipantā, durāsadā hi te Bhagavanto sīhā va ekacarā, yadā c'āhaɱ bho samaṇena Gotamena saddhiɱ manteyyaɱ, mā me bhonto, antar'antarā kathaɱ opātetha, kathā-pariyosānaɱ me bhavanto āgamentu" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Selo brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi, sammodaniyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇiyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Selo brāhmaṇo Bhagavato kāye dvattiɱsa mahā-purisa-lakkhanāni samannesi. Addasā kho Selo brāhmaṇo Bhagavato kāye dvattiɱsa mahāpuraghalakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve, dvisu mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇesu kankhati vici-kicchati nādhi-muccati na sampasidati, kosohite ca vatthaguyhe pahutajivhatāya ca.|| ||

Atha kho Bhagavato etad ahosi: "Passati kho me ayaɱ Selo brāhmaṇo dvittiɱsa mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇāni yebhuyyena ṭhapetvā dve, dvisu mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇesu kankhati vici-kicchati nādhi-muccati na sampasidati, kosohite ca vatthaguyhe pahutajivhatāya cā" ti. Atha kho Bhagavā tathā-rūpaɱ iddhābhisankhāraɱ abisaŋkhāsi yathā addasa Selo brāhmaṇo Bhagavato kosohitaɱ [108] vatthaguyhaɱ. Atha kho Bhagavā jivhaɱ ninnāmetvā ubho pi kaṇṇasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, ubho pi nāsikasotāni anumasi paṭimasi, kevalam pi nalāṭamaṇḍalaɱ jivhāya chadesi.|| ||

Atha kho Selassa brahmaṇassa etad ahosi: "Samannāgato kho samaṇo Gotamo dvattiɱsamahā-purisa-lakkhaṇehi paripuṇṇehi no aparipuṇṇehi, no ca kho naɱ jānāmi 'Buddho vā no vā.' Sutaɱ kho pana metaɱ brāhmaṇānaɱ vuddhānaɱ mahallakānaɱ ācariya-pācariyānaɱ bhāsa-mānānaɱ, 'Ye te bhavanti arahanto sammāSamBuddho te sake vaṇṇe bhaññamāne attānaɱ pātu-karonti' ti, yan nunāhaɱ samaṇaɱ Gotamaɱ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyan" ti. Atha kho Sele brāhmaṇo Bhagavantaɱ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

548. "Paripuṇṇakāyo suruci sujāto cārudasasano,||
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo si Bhagavā susukkadāṭho si viriyavā.|| ||

549. Narassa hi sujātassa ye bhavanti viyañajanā||
Sabb'ete tava kāyasmiɱ mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇā.|| ||

550. Pasannanetto sumukho brahā uju patāpavā,||
Majjhe samaṇaSaŋghassa ādicco va virocasi.|| ||

551. Kalyāṇadassano bhikkhu kañcanasannibhattaco,||
Kiɱ te samaṇabhāvena evaɱ uttamavaṇṇino.|| ||

552. Rājā arahasi bhavituɱ cakka-vatti rathesabho,||
Cāturanto vijitāvī Jambusaṇḍassa issaro.|| ||

[109] 553. Khattiyā bhoja-rājāno anuyuttā bhavatti te,||
Rājābhirājā manujindo rajjaɱ kārehi Gotama."|| ||

554. "Rājāham asmi Sela (iti Bhagavā ) Dhamma-rājā anuttaro,||
Dhammena cakkaɱ vattemi cakkaɱ appati-vattiyaɱ."|| ||

555. "SamBuddho paṭijānāsi (iti Selo brāhmaṇo) 'Dhamma-rājā anuttaro||
Dhammena cakkaɱ vattemi' ita bhāsasi Gotama.|| ||

556. Ko nu senāpita bhoto sāvako Satthu-d-anthayo,||
Ko te imaɱ anuvatteti Dhamma-cakkaɱ pavattitaɱ."|| ||

557. "Mayā pavattitaɱ cakkaɱ (Selā ti Bhagavā) Dhamma-cakkaɱ anuttaraɱ,||
Sāriputto anuvatteti anujāto Tathāgataɱ|| ||

558. Abhiññeyyaɱ abhiññātaɱ bhāvetabbañ ca bhāvitaɱ,||
Pahātabbaɱ pahinaɱ me, tasmā Buddho'smi brāhmaṇa|| ||

559. Vinayassu mayi kaŋkhaɱ adhimuccassu brāhmaṇa,||
Dullabhaɱ dassanaɱ hoti sambuddhānaɱ abhiṇhaso.|| ||

[110] 560. Yesaɱ vo dullabho loke pātu-bhāvo abhiṇahaso,||
So'haɱ brāhmaṇa sambudedhā salla-katto anuttaro|| ||

561. Brahmabhūto atitulo Mārasenappamaddano,||
Sabbāmitte vasikatvā modāmi akutobhayo."|| ||

562. "Imaɱ bhonto nisāmetha, yathā bhāsati cakkhumā,||
Sallakatto mahāvīro siho va nadati vane|| ||

563. Brahmabhūtaɱ atitulaɱ Mārasenappamaddanaɱ,||
Ko disvā na-ppasideyya api kaṇh'ābhijātiko.|| ||

564. Yo maɱ icchati anvetu, yo vā n'icchati gacchatu,||
Idh'āhaɱ pabbajissāmi varapaññassa santike."|| ||

565. "Etañ ce ruccati bhoto Sammā-Sam-Buddha-sāsanaɱ,||
Mayam pi pabbajissāma varapaññassa santike."|| ||

566. "Brāhmaṇā tisatā ime yā canti pañajalikatā,||
Buhmacariyaɱ carissāma Bhagavā tava santike."|| ||

567. "Svākkhātaɱ Brahma-cariyaɱ (Selā ti Bhagavā) sandiṭṭhikam akalikaɱ,||
Yattha amoghā pabbajjā appamattassa sikkhato" ti.|| ||

Alattha kho Selo brāhmaṇo sapariso Bhagavato santike pabbajjaɱ, alattha upasampadaɱ.|| ||

Atha kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo tassā rattiyā accayena sake assame paṇitaɱ khādaniyaɱ bhojaniyaɱ paṭiyādāpetvā [111] Bhagavato kālaɱ ārocāpasi: "Kālo bho Gotama niṭṭhitaɱ bhattan" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Bhagavā pubbanahasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacivaram ādāya yena Keṇiyassa jaṭilassa assamo ten'upasankami. Upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi, saddhiɱ bhikkhu-saŋghena. Atha kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo Buddha-pamukhaɱ bhikkhu-Saŋghaɱ paṇitena khādaniyena bhojaniyena sahatthā santappesi sampavāresi. Atha kho Keṇiyo jaṭilo Bhagavantaɱ bhuttāmiɱ onitapattapāṇiɱ aññataraɱ nicaɱ āsanaɱ gahetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Kheṇiyaɱ jaṭilaɱ Bhagavā imāhi gāthāhi anumodi.|| ||

568. "Aggihuttamukhā yaññā, Sāvitti chandaso mukhaɱ,||
Rājā mukhaɱ manussānaɱ, nadinaɱ sāgaro mukhaɱ.|| ||

569. Nakkhattānaɱ mukhaɱ cando, ādicco tapataɱ mukhaɱ,||
Puññaɱ ākaŋkha-mānānaɱ saŋgho ve yajataɱ mukhat" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Bhagavā Keṇiyaɱ jaṭilaɱ imāhi gāthāhi anumo-ditvā uṭṭhāy āsanā pakkāmi.|| ||

Atha kho āyasmā Selo sapariso eko vupakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpi pahit'atto viharatto na cirass'eva [112] yass'atthāya kula-puttā samma-d-eva agārasmā anagāriyaɱ pabbajanti. Tad anuttaraɱ Brahma-cariya-pariyosānaɱ diṭṭhe'va dhamme sayaɱ abhiññā sacchi-katvā upasampajja vihāsi.|| ||

Khiṇā jāti, vusitaɱ Brahma-cariyaɱ, kataɱ karaṇiyaɱ, nāparaɱ itthāntāyā' ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca kho pan'āyasmā Selo sapariyo arahataɱ ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho āyasmā Selo sapariso yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami. Upasaŋkamitvā ekaɱsaɱ cīvaraɱ katvā yena Bhagavā ten'añajalim paṇāmetvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi.|| ||

570. "Yaɱ taɱ saraṇam āgamma ito aṭṭhami cakkhuma,||
Sattarattena Bhagavā dant'ambha tava sāsane.|| ||

571. Tuvaɱ Buddho, tuvaɱ Satthā, tuvaɱ Mārābhābhu muni,||
Tuvaɱ anusaye chetvā tiṇṇo tāres'imaɱ pajaɱ.|| ||

572. Upadhi te samatikkantā, āsavā te padālitā,||
Siho si anupādāno pahiṇahayabheravo.|| ||

573. Bhikkhavo tisatā ime tiṭṭhanti pañajalikatā,||
Pāde cira pasārehi nāgā vandantu Satthuno" ti.|| ||

Sela Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

8. Salla Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

574. Animittam anaññātaɱ maccānaɱ idha jīvitaɱ kasirañ ca parittañ ca, tañ ca dukkhena saññutaɱ [113] 575. Na hi so upakkamo atthi, yena jātā na miyyare, jaram pi patvā maraṇam, evaɱ dhammā hi pāṇino. 576. Phalānam iva pakkānaɱ pāto papatanā bhayaɱ evaɱ jātānaɱ maccānaɱ niccaɱ maraṇato bhayaɱ 577. Yathā pi kumbhakārassa katā mattikabhājanā sabbe bhedanapariyantā, evam maccāna jivitaɱ 578. Dharā ca mahantā ca ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā sabbe maccuvasaɱ yanti, sabbe maccuparāyanā 579. Tesaɱ maccuparetānaɱ gacchataɱ paralokato na pitā tāyate puttaɱ ñātī vā pana ñātake. 580. Pekkhantaɱ yeva ñātīnaɱ passa lālapataɱ puthu ekameko va maccānaɱ go vajjho viya niyyati. 581. Evam abbhāhato loko maccunā ca jarāya ca, — tasmā dhīrā na socanti viditvā loka-pariyāyaɱ. 582. Yassa Maggaɱ na jānāsi āgatassa gatassa vā, ubhu ante asampassaɱ niratthaɱ paridevasi. 583. Paridevayamāno ce kañcid atthaɱ udabbahe sammūḷho hiɱsam attānaɱ, kayira c'enaɱ vicakkhaṇo. 584. Nahi ruṇṇena sokena santiɱ pappoti cetaso,||
Bhiyy'ass'uppajjate dukkhaɱ sarīraɱ upabhaññati.|| ||

[114] 585. Kiso vicaṇṇo bhavati hiɱsam attānam attatā,||
Na tena petā pālenti, niratthā paridevanā.|| ||

586. Sokam appajahaɱ jantu bhiyyo dukkhaɱ nigacchati,||
Anutthuṇanto kāla-kataɱ sokassa vasam anvagu.|| ||

587. Aññe pi passa gamine yathā-kammupage nare,||
Maccuno vasam āgamma phandante v'idha pāṇino.|| ||

588. Yena yena hi maññanti, tato taɱ hoti aññathā,||
Etādiso vinābhāvo, passa lokassa pariyāyaɱ.|| ||

589. Api ce vassa-sataɱ jive bhiyyo vā pana mānavo,||
Ñātisaŋghā vinā hoti, jānāti idha jīvitaɱ.|| ||

590. Tasmā arahato sutvā vineyya paridevitaɱ,||
Petaɱ kālekataɱ disvā 'na so labbhā mayā' iti.|| ||

591. Yathā saraṇam ādittaɱ vārinā parinibbaye,||
Evam pi dhīro sappañño paṇḍito kusalo naro||
Khippam uppatitaɱ sokaɱ vāto tulaɱ va dhaɱsaye.|| ||

592. Paridevaɱ pajappañ ca domanassañ ca attano,||
Attano sukham esāno abbahe sallam attano.|| ||

593. Abbūḷhasallo asito santiɱ pappuyya cetaso,||
Sabbasokaɱ atikkanto asoko hoti nibbuto ti.|| ||

Salla Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

[115]

 

9. Vāseṭṭha Suttaɱ

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Icchānŋgale viharati Icchānŋgalavana-saṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā abhiññātā brāhmaṇa-mahā-sālā Icchānŋgale paṭivasanti, seyyath'īdaɱ: Caŋki brāhmaṇo Tārukkho brāhmaṇo, Pokkharasāti brāhmaṇo Jānussoni bruhmaṇo Todeyya brāhmaṇo aññe ca abhiññātā abhiññatā brahmaṇamahāsāḷā. Atha kho Vāseṭṭha-Bhāradvājanaɱ māṇavānaɱ jaŋghā-vihāraɱ anucaŋkammānānaɱ anuvivaramānānaɱ ayam antarā kathā udapādi: "Kathaɱ bho brāhmaṇo hoti" ti.|| ||

Bhāradvājo māṇavo evam āha: "Yato kho bho ubhato sujāto hoti mātito ca pitito ca saɱsuddhagahaṇiko yāva sattamā pitā-mah'ayugā akkhitto anupakkuṭṭho jāti-vādena, ettāvatā kho brāhmaṇo hotī" ti.|| ||

Vāseṭṭho māṇavo evam āha: "Yato kho bho silavā ca hoti vatta-sampanno ca, ettāvatā kho brāhmaṇo hotī" ti. N'eva kho asakkhi Bhāradvājo māṇavo [116] Vāseṭṭhaɱ māṇavaɱ saññapetuɱ, na pana asakkhi Vāseṭṭho māṇavo Bhāradvājaɱ māṇavaɱ saññapetuɱ.|| ||

Atha kho Vāseṭṭho māṇavo Bhāradvājaɱ māṇavaɱ āmantesi: "Ayaɱ kho Bhāradvāja samaṇo Gotamo Sakya-putto Sakya-kulā pabba-jito Icchānŋgale viharati Icchānŋgalavana-saṇḍe, taɱ kho pana bhavannaɱ Gotamaɱ evaɱ kalyāṇo kitti-saddo abbhu-g-gato: itipi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāSamBuddho vijjācaranasampanne Sugato lovidu anuttaro purisa-dhamma-sārathi sāttā deva-manussānaɱ Buddho Bhagavāti. Āyāma bho Bhāradvāja, yena samaṇo Gotamo ten'upasankamissāma, upasankamitvā samaṇaɱ Gotamaɱ etam atthaɱ pucchissāma, yathā no samaṇo Gotamo vyākarissati, tathā naɱ dhāressāmā" ti. "Evaɱ bho" ti kho Bhāradvājo māṇavo Vāseṭṭhassa māṇavassa paccassosi.|| ||

Atha kho Visaṭṭha-Bhāradvājā māṇavā yena Bhagavā ten'upasankamiɱsu. Upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodiɱsu sammodaniyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇiyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdiɱsu. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Vāseṭṭho māṇavo Bhagavantaɱ gāthāhi ajjhābhāsi.|| ||

594. "Anuññātapaṭiññātā tevijjā mayam asm'ubho,||
Ahaɱ Pokkharasātissa Tārukkhassā'yaɱ māṇavo.|| ||

595. Tevijjānaɱ yad akkhātaɱ tatra kevalino smase,||
Padakā'asmā veyyā-karaṇā jape ācariyasādisā.|| ||

[117] 596. Tesaɱ no jātivādasmiɱ vivādo atthi Gotama,||
"Jātiyā brāhmaṇo hoti" Bhāradvājo iti bhāsati.||
Ahañ ca "Kammanā" brūmi, evaɱ jānāhi cakkhuma.|| ||

597. Te na Sakkoma saññattuɱ añña-maññaɱ mayaɱ ubho,||
Bhagavantaɱ puṭṭhum āgamma sambuddhaɱ iti vissutaɱ.|| ||

598. Candaɱ yathā khayātitaɱ pecca pañajalikā janā,||
Vandamānā namassanti evaɱ lokasmi Gotamaɱ.|| ||

599. Cakkhuɱ loke samuppannaɱ mayaɱ pucchāma Gotamaɱ,||
Jātiyā brāhmaṇo hoti udāhu bhavati kammanā;||
Ajānataɱ no pabrūhi, yathā jānemu brāhmaṇaɱ."|| ||

600. "Tesaɱ vo'haɱ vyakkhissaɱ (Vāseṭṭhā ti Bhagavā)||
anupubbaɱ yathātathaɱ||
Jātivibhāgaɱ pāṇānaɱ aññamaññā hi jātiyo.|| ||

601. Tiṇarukkha pi jānātha, na cāpi paṭijānare,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ, aññamaññā hi jātiyo.|| ||

[118] 602. Tato kīṭe paṭaŋge ca yāva kuntakipillike,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ aññamaññā hi jātiyo.|| ||

603. Catuppade pi jānātha khuddake ca mahallake,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ aññamaññā hi jātiyo.|| ||

604. Pādudare pi jānātha urage dighapiṭṭhike,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ añña-mañña hi jātiyo.|| ||

605. Tato macche pi jānātha odake vārigocare,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ aññamaññāhi jātiyo|| ||

606. Tato pakkhi pi jānātha pattayāne vibhaŋgame,||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ tesaɱ aññamaññā hi jātiyo.|| ||

607. Yathā etāsu jātisu liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ puthu,||
Evaɱ n'atthi manussesu liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ puthu."|| ||

608. Na kesehi na sisena na kaṇṇehi na akkhihi||
Na mukhena na nāsāya na oṭṭhehi bhamuhi vā.|| ||

609. Na givāya na aɱsehi na udarena na piṭṭhiyā,||
Na soniyā na urasā na sambādhe na methune.|| ||

610. Na hatthehi na pādehi nāŋgulīhi nakhehi vā,||
Na jaŋghāni na ūrūhi na vaṇṇena sarena va.||
Liŋgaɱ jātimayaɱ n'eva, yathā aññāsu jātisu.|| ||

[119] 611 Paccattaɱ sasarīresu manussesy-etaɱ na vijjati||
vokārañ ca manusesu samaññāya pavuccati.|| ||

612. Yo hi koci manussesu gorakkhaɱ upajīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, kassako so, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

613. Yo hi koci manussesu puthu sippena jīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, sippiko so, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

614. Yo hi koci manussesu vohāraɱ upajīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, vāṇijo so, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

615. Yo hi koci manussesu parapessena jīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, pessiko so, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

616. Yo hi koci manussesu adinnaɱ upajīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, coro eso, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

617. Yo hi koci manussesu issatthaɱ upajīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, yodhājivo, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

618. Yo hi koci manussesu porohiccena jīvati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, yājako so, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

619. Yo hi koci manussesu gāmaɱ raṭṭhañ ca bhuñjati,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭha jānāhi, rājā eso, na brāhmaṇo.|| ||

620. Na c'āhaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ brūmi yonijaɱ mattisambhavaɱ,||
Bhovādi nāma so hoti, sa ve hoti sakiñcano||
akiñcanaɱ anādānaɱ tam aham brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

621. Sabbasaŋyojanaɱ chetvā yo ve na paritassati,||
Saŋgātigaɱ visaɱyuttaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

[120] 622. Chetvā naddhiɱ varattañ ca sandānaɱ sahanukkamaɱ,||
Ukkhittapalighaɱ Buddhaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

623. Akkosaɱ vadhabandhañ ca aduṭṭho yo titikkhati,||
Khattibalaɱ balānikaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

624. Akkodhanaɱ vatavantaɱ silavantaɱ anussadaɱ,||
Dantaɱ antimasārīraɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

625. Vāri pokkharapatte va āragge-r-iva sāsapo,||
Yo na lippati kāmesu tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

626. Yo dukkhassa pajānāti idh'eva khayam attano,||
Pannabhāraɱ visaɱyuttaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

627. Gambhirapaññaɱ medhāviɱ Maggā-Maggassa kovidaɱ,||
Uttamatthaɱ anuppattaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

628. Asaɱsaṭṭhaɱ gahaṭṭhehi anāgārehi cubhayaɱ,||
Anokasāriɱ app'icchaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

629. Nidhāya daṇḍaɱ bhūtesu tasse thāvaresu ca,||
Yo na hanti na ghāteti tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

630. Aviruddhaɱ viruddhesu attadaṇḍesu nibbutaɱ,||
Sādānesu anādānaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

631. Yassa rāgo ca doso ca māno makkho ca pātito,||
Sāsapo-r-iva āraggā tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

[121] 632. Akkakasaɱ viññapaniɱ giraɱ saccaɱ udiraye,||
Yāya nābhisaje kañci tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

633. Yo ca dighaɱ va rassaɱ vā aṇuɱ thulaɱ subhāsubhaɱ,||
Loke adinnaɱ nādiyati tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

634. Āsā yassa na vijjanti asmiɱ loke parambhi ca,||
Nirāsayaɱ visaɱyuttaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

635. Yassālayā na vijjanti aññāya akathaɱ-kathī,||
Amatogadhaɱ anuppattaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

636. Yo'dha puññaɱ ca pāpāñ ca ubho saŋgaɱ upaccagā,||
Asokaɱ virajaɱ suddhaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

637. Candaɱ ca vimalaɱ suddhaɱ vippasannaɱ anāvilaɱ,||
Nandibhavaparikkhiṇaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

638. Yo imaɱ palipathaɱ duggaɱ saɱsāraɱ moham accagā,||
Tiṇṇo pāragato jhāyī anejo akathaɱ-kathi,||
Anupādāya nibbuto tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

639. Yo'dha kāme pahatvāna anāgāro paribbaje,||
Kāma-bhavaparikkhiṇaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

640. Yo'dha taṇhaɱ pahatvāna anāgāro paribbaje,||
Tanhābhavaparikkhiṇaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

641. Hitvā mānusakaɱ yogaɱ dibbaɱ yogaɱ upaccagā,||
Sabbayogavisaɱyuttaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

642. Hitvā ratiñ ca aratiñ ca sitibhūtaɱ nirūpadhiɱ,||
Sabba-lokāhibhuɱ viraɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

[122] 643. Cutiɱ yo vedi sattānaɱ upapattiñ ca sabbaso,||
Asattaɱ Sugataɱ Buddhaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

644. Yassa gatiɱ na jānanti devā gandhabbamānusā,||
Khiṇāsavaɱ arahantaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

645. Yassa pure ca pacchā ca majjhe ca n'atthi kiñcanaɱ,||
Akiñcanaɱ anādānaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

646. Usabhaɱ pavaraɱ viraɱ mahesiɱ vijitāvinaɱ,||
Anejaɱ nahātakaɱ Buddhaɱ tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ.|| ||

647. Pubbe-nivāsaɱ yo vedi saggāpāyañ ca passati,||
Atho jātikkhayaɱ patto, tam ahaɱ brūmi brāhmaṇaɱ|| ||

648. Samaññā h'esā lokasmiɱ nāmagottaɱ pakappitaɱ||
Sammuccā samudāgataɱ tattha tattha pakappitaɱ|| ||

649. Digharattam anusayitaɱ diṭṭhi-gatam ajānataɱ,||
Ajānantā no pabruvanti: "jātiyā hoti brāhmano"|| ||

650. Na jaccā brāhmaṇo hoti, na jaccā hoti abrāhmaṇo,||
Kammanā brāhmaṇo hoti, kammanā hoti abrāhmaṇo.|| ||

651. Kassako kammanā hoti, sippiko hoti kammanā,||
Vāṇijo kammanā hoti, pessiko hoti kammanā.|| ||

652. Coro pi kammanā hoti, yodhājivo pi kammanā,||
Yājako kammanā hoti rājā pi hoti kammanā.|| ||

[123] 653. Evam etaɱ yathā-bhūtaɱ kammaɱ passanti paṇḍitā,||
Paṭicca samuppādadasā kamma-vipākakovidā.|| ||

654. Kammānā vattati loko, kammanā vattati pajā,||
Kammanibandhanā sattā rathassāṇiva yāyato.|| ||

655. Tapena brahma-cariyena saɱyamena damena ca,||
Etena brāhmaṇo hoti, etaɱ brāhmaṇam uttamaɱ.|| ||

656. Tihi vijjāhi sampanno santo khiṇāpuna-b-bhavo,||
Evaɱ Vāseṭṭhi jānāhi, Brahmā Sakko vijānatan" ti.|| ||

Evaɱ vutte Vāseṭṭha-Bhāradvājā māṇavo Bhagavantaɱ etad avocuɱ: "Abhikkantaɱ bho goma seyyathā pibho Gotama, kikkujjitaɱ vā ukkujjeya, paṭi-c-channaɱ vā vivareyya, muḷhassavā Maggaɱ ācikkheyya, andha-kāre vā tela-pajjotaɱ dhāreyya cakkhu-manto rūpāni dakkhintiti, evam evaɱ bhotā Gotamena aneka-pariyāyena dhammo pakāsito, ete mayaɱ bhavantaɱ Gotamaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāma Dhammañ ca bhikkhu-Saŋghañca, upāsake no bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajja-t-agge pāṇupetaɱ- saraṇaɱ gatanti.|| ||

Vāseṭṭha Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

10. Kokāliya Suttaɱ

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍakassa ārāme atha kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhaga- [124] vantaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: || ||

"Pāpicchā bhante Sāriputta-Moggallānā pāpikānaɱ icchānaɱ vasaɱ gatā" ti. Evaɱ vutte Bhagavā Kokāliyaɱ bhikkhuɱ etad avoca: || ||

"Mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya, pasādehi Kokāliya Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ, pesalā Sāriputta-Moggallānā" ti.|| ||

Dutiyam pi kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kiñ cāpi me bhante Bhagavā saddhāyiko paccayiko, atha kho pāpicchā va Sāriputta-Moggallānā pāpikānaɱ icchānaɱ vasaɱ gatā" ti.|| ||

Dutiyam pi kho Bhagavā Kokāliyaɱ bhikkhuɱ etad avoca: "Mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya pāsadehi Kokāliya Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ, pesalā Sāriputta-Moggallānā" ti.|| ||

Tatiyam pi kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kiñ cāpi me bhante Bhagavā saddhāyiko paccayiko, atha kho pāpicchā va Sāriputta-Moggallānā pāpikānaɱ icchānaɱ vasaɱ gatā" ti.|| ||

Tatiyam pi kho Bhagavā Kokāliyaɱ bhikkhuɱ etad avoca: "Mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya mā h'evaɱ Kokāliya pāsadehi Kokāliya Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ, pesalā Sāriputta-Moggallānā" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu uṭṭhāy āsanā Bhagavantaɱ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā pakkāmi. Acira-pakkantassa ca Kokāliyassa bhikkhuno sāsapa-mattihi piḷakāhi sabbo kāyo phuṭho ahosi. Sāsapamattiyo hutvā mugga-mattiyo ahesuɱ. Mugga-mattiyo hutvā kaḷāyamattiyo ahesuɱ. Kaḷāyamattiyo hutvā kolaṭṭhi-mattiyo ahesuɱ. [125] Kolaṭṭhi-mattiyo hutvā kola-mattiyo ahesuɱ. Kola-mattiyo hutvā āmalaka-mattiyo ahesuɱ. Āmalaka-mattiyo hutvā beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo ahesuɱ beḷuvasalāṭukamattiyo hutvā billa-mattiyo ahesuɱ. Billa-mattiyo hutvā pabhijjiɱsu, pubbañ ca lohitañ ca pagaghariɱsu.|| ||

Atha kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu ten'evabādhena kālam akāsi, kāla-kato ca kho Kokāliyo bhikkhu Paduma Nirayaɱ upapajji Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ āghātetvā.|| ||

Atha kho Brahmā Sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkanta vaṇṇo kevala-kappaɱ Jetavanaɱ obhāsetvā yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavantaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi. Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhito kho Brahmā Sahampati Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kokāliyo bhante bhikkhu kāla-kato. Kālakato ca bhante Kokāliyo bhikkhu PadumaNirayaɱ upapanno Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ āghātetvā" ti. Idam avoca Brahmā Sahampati, idaɱ vatvā Bhagavantaɱ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā tatth'ev'antara-dhāyi.|| ||

Atha kho Bhagavā tassa rattiyā accayena bhikkhu āmantesi: "Imaɱ bhikkhave rattiɱ Brahmā Sahampati abhikkannāya rattiyā abhikkanta vaṇṇo kevala-kappaɱ Jetavanaɱ obhāsetvā yena Bhagavā ten'upasankami, upasankamitvā Bhagavantaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi. Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhito kho Brahmā Sahampati Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kokāliyo bhante bhikkhu kāla-kato. Kālakato ca bhante Kokāliyo bhikkhu PadumaNirayaɱ upapanno Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ āghātetvā" ti. Idam avoca Brahmā Sahampati, idaɱ vatvā maɱ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaɱ katvā tatth'ev'antara-dhāyi" ti.|| ||

Evaɱ vutte aññataro bhikkhu [126] Bhagavantaɱ etad avoca: "Kivadighaɱ nu kho bhante Padume Niraye āyu-p-pamāṇan" ti?|| ||

"Dīghaɱ kho bhikkhu Padume Niraye āyu-p-pamāṇaɱ, taɱ na sukaraɱ saŋkhātuɱ ettakāni vassāni iti vā 'ettakāni vassa-satāni' iti vā 'ettakāni vassa-sahassāni' iti vā 'ettakāni vassa-sata-sahassāni' iti vā" ti.|| ||

"Sakkā pana bhante upamaɱ kātun" ti?|| ||

"Sakkā bhikkhunī" Bhagavā avoca: "Seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati khāriko Kosalako tivalavāho, tato puriso vassa-satassa vassa-satassa accayena ekam ekaɱ tilaɱ uddhareyya, khippataraɱ kho so bhikkhu visati khāriko Kosalako tilavāho iminā upakkamena parikkhayaɱ pariyādānaɱ gaccheyya, na tv'eva eko Abbudo Nirayo. Seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Abbudā Nirayā evam eko Nirabbudo Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Nirabbudā Nirayā evam eko Ababo Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Ababā Nirayā evam eko Ahaho Nirayo. Seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Ahahā Nirayā evam eko Aṭaṭo Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Aṭaṭā Nirayā evam eko Kumudo Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Kumudā Nirayā evam eko Sogandhiko Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Sogandhikā Nirayā evam eko Uppalako Nirayo, sayyethā pi bhikkhu visati Uppalakā Nirayā evam eko Puṇḍariko Nirayo, seyyathā pi bhikkhu visati Puṇḍarikā Nirayā evam eko Padumo Nirayo. Padumaɱ kho pana bhikkhu Nirayaɱ Kokāliyo bhikkhu upapanno Sāriputta-Moggallānesu cittaɱ āghātetvā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā, idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

[127] 657. "Purisassa hi jātassa kuṭhāri jāyate mukhe,||
Yāya chindati attānaɱ bālo dubbhāsitaɱ bhaṇaɱ.|| ||

658. Yo nindiyaɱ pasaɱsati||
taɱ vā nindati yo pasaɱsiyo,||
Vicināti mukhena so kaliɱ||
kalinā tena sukhaɱ na vindati.|| ||

659. Appamatto ayaɱ kali,||
yo akkhesu dhana parājayo,||
Sabbassāpi sahāpi attanā||
ayam eva mahattaro kali,||
Yo sugatesu manaɱ padosaye.|| ||

660. Sataɱ sahassānaɱ Nirabbudānaɱ||
Chattiɱsa ca pañca ca Ababudāni,||
Yam ariyagarahi Nirayaɱ upeti||
Vācaɱ manañ ca paṇidhāya pāpakaɱ.|| ||

661. Abhūtavādi Nirayaɱ upeti||
Yo vā pi katvā "na karomī" ti cāha,||
Ubho pi te pecca samā bhavanti||
Nihinakammā manujā parattha.|| ||

662. Yo appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati||
Suddhassa posassa anaŋgaṇassa,||
Tam eva bālaɱ pacceti pāpaɱ||
Sukhumo rājo paṭivātaɱ va khitto.|| ||

663. Yo lobhaguṇe anuyutto||
So vacasā paribhāsati aññe,||
[128] Assaddho kadariyo avadaññu||
Macchari pesuniyasmiɱ anuyutto.|| ||

664. Mukhadugga vibhūta-m-anariya||
Bhunahu pāpaka dukkatakāri,||
Purisanta kali avajāta||
Mā bahu bhāṇ'idha nerayiko'si.|| ||

665. Rajam ākirasi abhitāya||
Sante garahasi kibbisakāri,||
Bahuni ca du-c-caritāni caritvā||
Gañachisi kho papataɱ cirarattaɱ|| ||

666. Na hi nassati kassaci kammaɱ||
Iti ha taɱ labhat'eva suvāmi,||
Dukkhaɱ mando para-loke||
Attani passati kibbisakāri.|| ||

667. Ayosaɱkusamāhataṭṭhānaɱ||
Tiṇahadhāraɱ ayasulam upeti,||
[129] Atha tatta ayo guḷasannibhaɱ||
Bhojanam atthi tathā patirūpaɱ.|| ||

668. Na hi vaggu vadanti vadantā||
Nābhijavanti na tāṇam upenti,||
Aŋgāre santhate senti||
Agginisamaɱ jalitaɱ pavisanti.|| ||

669. Jālena ca onahiyānā||
Tattha hananti ayomayakuṭehi,||
Andhaɱ va timisam āyanti||
Taɱ vitataɱ hi yathā mahikāyo.|| ||

670. Atha lohamayaɱ pana kumbhiɱ||
Agginisamaɱ jalitaɱ pavisanti,||
Paccanti hi tāsu cirarattaɱ||
Agginisamāsu samuppilavāso.|| ||

671. Atha pubbalohitamisse||
Tattha kiɱ paccati kibbisakārī,||
[130] Yaɱ ñaɱ disataɱ adhiseti||
Tattha kilijjati samaphusamāno.|| ||

672. Puḷavāvasathe salilasmiɱ||
Tattha kiɱ paccati kibbisakāri,||
Ganatuɱ na hi tiram ap'atthi||
Sabbasamā hi samantakapallā.|| ||

673. Asipattavanaɱ pana tiṇhaɱ||
Taɱ pavisanti samacchidagattā,||
Jivhaɱ baḷisena gahetvā||
Āracayā racayā vihananti.|| ||

674. Atha Vetaraṇiɱ pana duggaɱ||
Tiṇhadhāra khuradhāram upenti,||
Tattha mandā papatanti||
Pāpakarā pāpāni karitvā.|| ||

[131] 675. Khādanti hi tattha rudante||
Sāmā sabalā kākolagaṇā ca,||
Soṇā sigālā paṭigijjhā||
Kulalā vāyasā ca vitudanti.|| ||

676. Kicchā vatāyaɱ idha vutti||
Yaɱ jano passati kibbisakāri,||
Tasmā idha jīvitasese||
Kiccakāro siyā naro na ca majje.|| ||

677. Te gaṇitā viduhi tilavāhā||
ye Padume Niraye upanitā,||
Nahutāni hi koṭiyo pañca bhavanti||
Dvādasa koṭi satāni pun'aññā.|| ||

678. Yāva-dukkhā Nirayā idha vuttā||
Tatthā pi tāva ciraɱ vasitabbaɱ,||
Tasmā suci pesala sādhu guṇesu||
Vācaɱ manaɱ satataɱ parirakkhe" ti.|| ||

Kokāliya Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

11. Nālaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

679. Ānandajāte tidasagaṇe patīte||
Sakkacca Indaɱ sucivasane ca deve,||
Dussaɱ gahetvā atiriva thomayante||
Asito isi addasa divā-vihāre.|| ||

[132] 680. Disvāna deve muditamane udagge||
Cittiɱ karitvā idam avocāsi tattha,||
"Kiɱ devasaŋgho atiriva kalyarūpo||
Dussaɱ gahetvā bhamayatha kiɱ paṭicca.|| ||

681. Yadā pi āsi asurehi saŋgamo||
Jayo surānaɱ Asurā parājitā,||
Tadā pi n'etādiso lomahaɱsano||
Kiɱ abbhutaɱ daṭṭhu marū pamoditā.|| ||

682. Seḷenti gāyanti ca vādayanti ca||
Bhujāni poṭhenti ca naccayanti ca,||
Pucchāmi vo'haɱ Merumuddhavāsine||
Dhunātha me saɱsayaɱ khippa mārisā."|| ||

683. "So Bodhisatto ratanavaro atulyo||
Manusseloke hitasukhatāya jāto,||
Sakyānaɱ game jana-pade Lumbineyye||
Ten'ambha tuṭṭhā atiriva kalyarūpā.|| ||

684. So sabbasattuttamo aggapuggalo||
Narāsabho sabbapajānam uttamo,||
[133] Vattessati cakkaɱ Isivahaye vane||
Nadaɱ va siho balavā migādhibhū.|| ||

685. Taɱ saddaɱ sutvā turitam avaɱsari so||
Suddhodanassa tadā bhavanaɱ upāgami,||
Nisajja tatthu idam avocāsi Sakye||
"Kuhiɱ kumāro aham api daṭṭhukāmo.|| ||

686. Tato kumāraɱ jalitam iva suvaṇṇaɱ||
Ukkāmukhe va sukusalasampahaṭṭhaɱ,||
Daddallamānaɱ siriyā anomavaṇṇaɱ||
Dassesu puttaɱ Asitavahayassa Sakyā.|| ||

687. Disvā kumāraɱ sikhim iva pajjalantaɱ||
Tārāsabhaɱ va nabhasigamaɱ visuddhaɱ,||
Suriyaɱ tapantaɱ sarada-r-iv'abbhamuttaɱ||
Ānandajato vipulam alattha pitiɱ.|| ||

688. Anekapākhañ ca sahassamaṇḍalaɱ||
Chattaɱ marū dhārayum antalikkhe,||
Suvaṇṇadaṇḍā vitipatanti cāmarā||
Na dissare cāmarachatatagāhakā.|| ||

[134] 689. Disvā jaṭī Kaṇhasirivahayo isi||
Suvaṇṇanekkhaɱ viya paṇḍukambale,||
Setañ ca chattaɱ dhariyanta muddhani||
Udaggacitto sumano paṭiggahe.|| ||

690. Paṭiggahetvā pana Sakyapuŋgavaɱ||
Jigiɱsako lakkhaṇamantapāragu,||
Pasannacitto giram abbhudīrayi||
"Anuttar'āyaɱ dipadānam uttamo".|| ||

691. Ath'attano gamanam anussaranto||
Akalyarūpo galayati assukāni,||
Disvāna Sakyā isim avocuɱ rudantaɱ||
"No ce kumāre bhavisti antarāyo."|| ||

692. Disvāna Sakeye isi-m-avoca akalye||
"Nāhaɱ kumāre ahitam anussarāmi,||
Na cāpi-m-assa bhavissati antarāyo||
Na orak'ayaɱ adhimānasā bhavātha.|| ||

693. Sambodhiyaggaɱ phusissat'āyaɱ kumāro||
So Dhamma-cakkaɱ paramavisuddhadassi,||
Vattessat'āyaɱ bahu-jana-hitānukampi||
Vitthārik'assa bhavissati Brahma-cariyaɱ.|| ||

[135] 694. Mamañ ca āyu na ciram idhāvaseso||
Ath'anatarā me bhavissati kāla-kiriyā,||
So'haɱ na sussaɱ asamadhurassa dhammaɱ||
Ten'amhi aṭṭo vyasanagato aghāvi."|| ||

695. So Sākiyānaɱ vipulaɱ janetvā pitiɱ||
Antepurambhā niragamā brahma-cāri,||
So bhāgineyyaɱ sayam anukampamāno||
Samādapesi asamadhurassa dhamme.|| ||

696. "'Buddho' ti ghosaɱ yada parato suṇāsi||
'Sambodhipatto vicarati dhammaMaggaɱ,||
Gantvāna tattha samayaɱ paripucchiyāno||
Carassu tasmiɱ Bhagavati brahama-cariyaɱ.|| ||

697. Tenānusiṭṭho hitamanasena tādinā||
Anāgate paramavisuddhadassinā,||
So Nāḷako upacitapuññasañcayo||
Jinaɱ patikkhaɱ parivasi rakkhitindriyo.|| ||

698. Sutvāna ghosaɱ Jinavaracakka-vattane||
Gantvāna disvā isinisabhaɱ pasanno,||
[136] Moneyyaseṭṭhaɱ munipavaraɱ apucchi||
Samāgate asitavahayassa sāsane ti.|| ||

Vatthugāthā.|| ||

699. "Aññātam etaɱ vacanaɱ Asitassa yathātathaɱ||
Taɱ taɱ Gotama pucchāma sabba-dhammāna pāraguɱ.|| ||

700. Anagāriy'upetassa bhikkhacariyaɱ jigiɱ-sato,||
Muni pabrūhi me puṭṭho moneyyaɱ uttamaɱ padaɱ."|| ||

701. "Moneyyaɱ te apaññissaɱ (iti Bhagavā)||
Dukkaraɱ du-r-abhisambhavaɱ,||
Handa te naɱ pavakkhāmi santhambhassu daḷho bhava.|| ||

702. Samānabhāvaɱ kubbetha gāme akkuṭṭhavanditaɱ,||
Manopadosaɱ rakkheyya santo anunnato care.|| ||

[137] 703. Uccāvacā niccharanti dāye aggisikhupamā,||
Nāriyo muniɱ palobhenti tā su taɱ mā palobhayuɱ.|| ||

704. Virato methunā dhammā hitvā kāme parocare.||
Aviruddho asāratto pāṇesu tasathāvare|| ||

705. 'Yathā ahaɱ tathā ete yathā ete tathā ahaɱ,'||
Attānaɱ upamaɱ katvā na haneyya na ghātaye.|| ||

706. Hitvā icchañ ca lobhañ ca yattha satto puthujjano,||
Cakkhumā paṭipajjeyya tareyya narakaɱ imaɱ.|| ||

707. Ūnūdaro mitāhāro apapicch'assa alolupo,||
Sa ve icchāya nicchāto aniccho hoti nibbuto.|| ||

708. Sa piṇḍacāraɱ caritvā vanantam abhihāraye,||
Upaṭṭhito rukkhamulasmiɱ āsanupagato muni.|| ||

709. Sa jhānapasuto dhīro vanante ramito siyā,||
Jhāyetha rukkhamulasmiɱ attānam abhitosayaɱ.|| ||

710. Tato ratyā vivasane gāmantam abhihāraye,||
Avhānaɱ nābhitandeyya abhihārañ ca gāmato.|| ||

711. Na muni gāmam āgamma kulesu sahasā care,||
Ghāsesanaɱ chinnakatho na vācaɱ payutaɱ bhaṇe.|| ||

712. 'Alatthaɱ yad idaɱ sādhu nālatthaɱ kusalaɱ iti,||
Ubhayen'eva so tādi rukkhaɱ va upanivattati.|| ||

[138] 713. Sa pattapāṇi vicaranto amugo mugasammato,||
Appaɱ dānaɱ na hīḷeyya dātāraɱ nāvajāniya.|| ||

714. Uccāvacā hi paṭipadā samaṇena pakāsitā,||
Na pāraɱ diguṇaɱ yanti na idaɱ ekaguṇaɱ mutaɱ.|| ||

715. Yassa ca visatā n'atthi chinnasotassa bhikkhuno,||
Kiccākiccappahīnassa pariḷāho na vijjati.|| ||

716. Moneyyaɱ te upaññissaɱ (iti Bhagavā)||
Khuradhārūpamo bhave,||
Jivahāya tāluɱ āhacca udare saññato siyā.|| ||

717. Alinacitto ca sipā na cāpi bahu cintaye,||
Nirāmagandho asito Brahma-cariyaparāyano.|| ||

718. Ekāsanassa sikkhethakha samaṇupāsanassa ca,||
Ekattaɱ monam akkhātaɱ eko ce abhiramissati.|| ||

719. Atha bhāsihi dasa disā||
Sutvā dhīrānaɱ nigghosaɱ jhāyīnaɱ kāmacāginaɱ,||
Tato hiriñ ca saddhañ ca bhiyyo kubbetha māmako.|| ||

[139] 720. Taɱ nadihi vijānātha sobebhasu padaresu ca,||
Saṇantā yanti kussobbhā tuṇahi yāti mahodayi.|| ||

721. Yad unakaɱ taɱ saṇati yaɱ puraɱ sattam eva taɱ,||
Aḍḍhakumbhūpamo bālo rahado puro va paṇḍito|| ||

722. Yaɱ samaṇo bahu bhāsati upetaɱ attha-saɱhitaɱ,||
Jānaɱ so dhammaɱ deseti jānaɱ so bahu bhāsati.|| ||

723. Yo ca jānaɱ yatatto jānaɱ na bahu bhāsati,||
Sa muni monam arahati sa muni monam ajjhā" ti.|| ||

Nālaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ.|| ||

 

 

12. Dvayatanupassana Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Pubb-ā-rāme Migāra-mātu pāsāde. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā tadah'uposathe pannarase puṇṇāya puṇṇamāya rattiyā bhikkhu-Saŋgha parivuto abbhokāse nisinno[140] hoti. Atha kho Bhagavā tuṇhibhūtaɱ tuṇhibhūtaɱ bhikkhu-Saŋghaɱ anuciloketvā bhikkhu āmantesi:|| ||

"'Ye te bhikkhave, kusalā dhammā ariyā niyyānikā sambodha gāmino, tesaɱ vo bhikkhave, kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ariyānaɱ niyyānikānaɱ sambodha-gāminaɱ kā upanisā savaṇāyā' ti. Iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, te evam assu vacaniyā: 'yāva-d-eva dvayatānaɱ dhammānaɱ yathā-bhūtaɱ ñāṇāyā' ti.|| ||

Kiñ ca dvayataɱ vadetha?|| ||

'Idaɱ dukkhaɱ, ayaɱ dukkha-samudayo' ti ayam ekānupassanā, 'ayaɱ dukkha-nirodho, ayaɱ dukkha-nirodha-gāminipaṭipadā' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

724. "Ye dukkhaɱ na-ppajānanti atho dukkhassa sambhavaɱ||
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaɱ asesaɱ uparujjhati,||
Tañ ca Maggaɱ na jānanti dukkhupasama-gāminaɱ.|| ||

725. Cetovimuttihinā te atho paññā-vimuttiyā,||
Ahabbā te antakiriyāya, te ve jātijarūpagā.|| ||

726. Ye ca dukkhaɱ pajānanti atho dukkhassa sambhavaɱ,||
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaɱ asesaɱ uparujjhati,||
[141] Tañ ca Maggaɱ pajānanti dukkhupasama-gāminaɱ.|| ||

727. Cetovimutti-sampannā atho paññā-vimuttiyā,||
Bhabbā te antakiriyāya, na te jātijarupagā" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ upadhipaccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'upādhinaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

728. "Upadhinidhānā pabhavanti dukkhā||
Ye keci lokasmiɱ anakarūpā,||
Yo ve avidvā upadhiɱ karoti.||
Punappunaɱ dukkham upeti mando,||
Tasmā pajānaɱ upadhiɱ na kayirā||
Dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassi" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ avijjā-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'avijjāya tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

[142] 729. Jātimaraṇasaɱsāraɱ ye vajanti puna-p-punaɱ,||
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaɱ, avijjāy'eva sā gati.|| ||

730. Avijjā h'ayaɱ mahāmoho yen'idaɱ saɱsitaɱ ciraɱ,||
Vijjāgatā ca ye sattā, nāga-c-chanti puna-b-bhavan" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ sankhāra-paccayāti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'sankhārānaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

731. "'Yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti, sabbaɱ sankhāra-paccayā,||
Saŋkharānaɱ nirodhena n'atthi dukkhassa gambhavo' ti.|| ||

732. Etam ādinavaɱ ñatvā 'dukkhaɱ sankhāra-paccayā',||
Sabba-sankhāra-samathā saññāya uparodhanā,||
Evaɱ dukkha-k-khayo hoti, etaɱ ñatvā yathātathaɱ.|| ||

733. Sammaddasā vedaguno samma-d-aññāya paṇḍitā,||
Abhibhuyya Mārasaɱyogaɱ nāga-c-chanti puna-b-bhavan" ti.|| ||

[143] "'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ viññāṇa-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'viññāṇassa tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

734. "Yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti, sabbaɱ viññāṇa-paccayā,||
Viññāṇassa nirodhena n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo.|| ||

735. Etam ādinaɱ ñatvā 'dukkhaɱ viññāṇa-paccayā',||
Viññāṇupasamā bhikkhu nicchāto parinibbuto" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ phassa-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'phassassa tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

736. "Tesaɱ phassa-paretānaɱ bhavasotānusārinaɱ,||
Kummagga-paṭipannānaɱ ārā saŋyojanakkhayo.|| ||

737. Ye ca phassaɱ pariññāya aññāya upasame ratā,||
Te ve phassābhisamayā nicchātā parinibbutā" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ vedanā-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'vedanānaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

[144] 738. "Sukhaɱ vā yadi vā dukkhaɱ adukkha-m-asukhaɱ saha||
Ajjhattañ ca bahiddhā ca yaɱ kiñci atthi veditaɱ,|| ||

739. Etaɱ 'dukkhan' ti ñatvāna mosadhammaɱ palokitaɱ||
Phussa phussa vayaɱ passaɱ evaɱ tatthi vijānāti||
Vedanānaɱ khayā bhikkhu nicchāto parinibbuto" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ taṇhā-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, taṇhāya tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhevo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

740. "Taṇhā dutiyo puriso digham addhānaɱ saɱsaraɱ,||
Itthābhāvaññathābhāvaɱ saɱsāraɱ nāti-vattati.|| ||

741. Etam ādinaɱ ñatvā taṇhā dukkhassa sambhavaɱ;||
Vitataṇho anādāno sato bhikkhu paribbaje" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ upādāna-paccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'upādhinaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

742. "Upādānaɱpaccayā bhavo, bhūto dukkhaɱ nigacchati,||
Jātassa maraṇaɱ hoti, eso dukkhassa sambhavo.|| ||

743. Tasmā upādānakkhayā samma-d-aññāya paṇḍitā,||
Jātikkhayaɱ abhiññāya nāga-c-chanti puna-b-bhavan" ti.|| ||

[145] "'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ ārampaccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'arambhānaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

744. "Yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti, sabbaɱ ārambhapaccayā,||
Ārambhānaɱ nirodhena n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo.|| ||

745. Etam ādinavaɱ ñatvā ārambhapaccayā,||
Sabbārambhaɱ paṭinissajja anārambha-vimuttino|| ||

746. Ucchinnabhavataṇhassa santa-cittassa bhikkhuno,||
Vitiṇṇo jāti-saɱsāro, n'atthi tassa puna-b-bhavo" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ āhārapadhipaccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'āhārānaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

747. "Yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti, sabbaɱ ārambhapaccayā,||
Āhārānaɱ nirodhena n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo.|| ||

748. Etam ādinavaɱ ñatvā 'dukkhaɱ āhārapaccayā',||
Sabbāhāram pariññāya sabbāhāram anissito.|| ||

[146] 749. Ārogyaɱ samma-d-aññāya āsavānaɱ parikkhayā,||
Saŋkhāya sevi dhammaṭṭho saŋkhaɱ na upeti vedagu" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti. Sabbaɱ iñajitapaccayā' ti, ayam ekānupassanā, 'iñajitānaɱ tv-eva asesa-virāga-nirodhā n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

750. "Yaɱ kiñci dukkhaɱ sambhoti, sabbaɱ iñjitapaccayā,||
Iñajitānaɱ nirodhena n'atthi dukkhassa sambhavo.|| ||

751. Etam ādinavaɱ ñatvā 'dukkhaɱ iñajitapaccayā',||
Tasmā ejaɱ vossajja sankhāre uparundhiya,||
Anejo anupādāno sato bhikkhu paribbaje" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'nissitassa calitaɱ hoti' ti ayam ekānupassanā, 'anissato na calati' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

752. "Anisasito na calati, nissito ca upādiyaɱ,||
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaɱ saɱsāraɱ nātavattati.|| ||

753. Etam ādinava ñatvā 'nissayesu mahabbhayaɱ',||
Anissito anupādāno sato bhikkhu paribbaje" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, 'siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'rūpehi bhikkhave āruppā statatarā' ti ayam ekānupassanā, [147] 'ārūppehi nirodho sattataro' ti ayaɱ dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

754. "Ye ca rūpupagā sattā ye va āruppavāsino||
Nirodhaɱ appajānantā āgantāro puna-b-bhavaɱ|| ||

755. Ye ca rūpe pariññāya arupesu susaṇṭhitā,||
Nirodhe ye vimuccanti, to jana maccuhāyino" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ bhikkhave sa-devakassa lokassa sa-mārakassa sa-s-samaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadeva-manussāya 'idaɱ saccan' ti upanijjhāyitaɱ, tadam ariyānaɱ 'etaɱ musā' ti yathā-bhūtaɱ samma-ppaññāya su-diṭṭhaɱ, ayam ekānupassanā, yaɱ bhikkhave sa-devakassa lokassa sa-mārakassa sa-s-samaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadeva-manussāya 'idaɱ saccan' ti upanijjhāyitaɱ, tadam ariyānaɱ 'etaɱ musā' ti yathā-bhūtaɱ samma-ppaññāya su-diṭṭhaɱ, ayam dutiyānupassanā. Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

756. "Anattani attamāniɱ passa lokaɱ sa-devakaɱ,||
Niviṭṭhaɱ nāma-rūpasmiɱ, 'idaɱ saccan' ti maññati.|| ||

757. Yena yena hi maññanti, tato taɱ hoti aññathā,||
Taɱ hi tassa musā hoti, mosadhammaɱ hi ittaraɱ.|| ||

[148] 758. Amosadhammaɱ Nibbānaɱ tad ariyā saccuto vidu,||
Te ve saccābhisamayā nicchātā parinibbutā" ti.|| ||

"'Siyā aññena pi pariyāyena sammā-dvayatānupasasnā' ti iti ce bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, siyā' ti'ssu vacaniyā, kathañ ca siyā: 'yaɱ bhikkhave sa-devakassa lokassa sa-mārakassa sa-s-samaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadeva-manussāya 'idaɱ saccan' ti upanijjhāyitaɱ, tadam ariyānaɱ 'etaɱ dukkhan' ti yathā-bhūtaɱ samma-ppaññāya su-diṭṭhaɱ, ayam ekānupassanā, yaɱ bhikkhave sa-devakassa lokassa sa-mārakassa sa-s-samaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadeva-manussāya 'idaɱ dukkhan' ti upanijjhāyitaɱ, tadam ariyānaɱ 'etaɱ sukhan' ti yathā-bhūtaɱ samma-ppaññāya su-diṭṭhaɱ, ayam dutiyānupassanā.|| ||

Evaɱ sammā-dvayatānupassino kho bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpito pahit'attassa viharato dvinnaɱ phalānaɱ aññataraɱ phalaɱ pāṭikaŋkhaɱ: diṭṭhe'va dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese Anāgāmitā" ti. Idam avoca Bhagavā idaɱ vatvā Sugato athāparaɱ etad avoca Satthā:|| ||

759. "Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā phassā dhammā ca kevalā,||
Iṭṭhā kantā manāpā ca, yāvat' 'atthi' ti vuccati.|| ||

760. Sadevakassa lokassa ete vo sukhasammatā,||
Yathā c'ete nirujjhanti, taɱ tesaɱ dukkhasammataɱ.|| ||

761. 'Sukhan' ti diṭṭham ariyehi sakkāyass'uparodhanaɱ,||
Paccanikam idaɱ hoti sabba-lokena passataɱ|| ||

[149] 762. Yaɱ pare sukhato āhu, tad ariyā āhu dukkhato,||
Yaɱ pare dukkhato āhu tad ariyā sukhato vidu,||
Passa dhammaɱ durājānaɱ, sampamuḷh'ettha aviddasu,|| ||

763. Nivutānaɱ tamo hoti, andhakāro apassataɱ,||
Satañ ca vivaṭaɱ hoti āloko passatām iva,||
Santike na vijānanti magā dhammass'akovidā.|| ||

764. Bhava-rāgaparetehi bhavasotānusārihi,||
Māradheyyānupattehi nāyaɱ dhammo susamabudho.|| ||

765. Ko nu aññatra-m-ariyehi padaɱ sambuddhum arahati,||
Yaɱ padaɱ samma-d-aññaya parinibbanti anāsavā" ti.|| ||

Idam avoca Bhagavā. Attamanā te bhikkhu Bhagavato bhāsitaɱ abhinandun. Imasmiɱ kho pana veyyā-karaṇasmiɱ bhaññamāne saṭṭhittānaɱ bhikkhunaɱ anupādāya āsavehi cittāni vimucciɱsuti.|| ||

Dvayatānupassanā Suttaɱ niṭṭitaɱ

[150] Tass'uddānaɱ:||
Saccaɱ upadhi avijjā ca sankhāra viññāṇapañcamaɱ,||
Phassa-vedaniyā taṇhā upādānaramhā āhārā;||
Iñijite phanditaɱ rūpaɱ sacca-dukkhena soḷasā ti.||
Mahāvaggo tatiyo.|| ||

Tassavaggassuddānaɱ:||
Pabbajjāñ ca Padhānañ ca Subhāsitañ ca Puraḷāsaɱ||
Māgha Suttañ ca Sabhiyo ca Selo Sallaɱ pavuccati,||
Vāseṭṭho cāpi Kokāli Nālako Dvayatānupassanā,||
dvādas'etāni suttāni Mahāvaggo ti vuccati ti.|| ||

 

[151]

IV. Aṭṭhaka Vagga

Proofed against the P.T.S. 2010 printing of the Dines Andersen and Helmer Smith 1913 edition.

 

 

1. Kāma Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

766. Kāmaɱ kāmayamānassa tassa ce taɱ samijjhati,||
Addhā pitimano hoti laddhā macco yad icchati.|| ||

767. Tassa ce kāmayānassa chanda-jātassa janatuno,||
Te kāmā parihāyanti, sallaviddho va ruppati.|| ||

768. Yo kāme parivajjeti sappass'eva padā siro,||
So imaɱ visattikaɱ loke sato samativattati|| ||

769. Khettaɱ vatthuɱ hiraññaɱ vā gavāssaɱ dāsaporisaɱ||
Thiyo bandhu puthu kāme yo nāro anugijjhati.|| ||

770. Abalā naɱ baliyanti, maddatte naɱ parissayā,||
Tato naɱ dukkham anveti nāvaɱ bhinnam ivōdakaɱ|| ||

771. Tasmā janatu sadā sato kāmāni parivajjaye,||
Te pahāya tare oghaɱ nāvaɱ siñcitva pāragu ti.|| ||

Kāma Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

2. Guhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

772. Satto guhāyaɱ bahunābhichanno||
Tiṭṭhaɱ naro mohanasmiɱ pagāḷho,||
[152] Dure vivekā hi tathāvidho so||
Kāmā hi loke na hi suppahāyā.|| ||

773. Icchānidānā bhavasātabaddhā||
Te duppamuñcā, na hi aññamokkhā,||
Pacchā pure vā pi apekkhamānā||
Ime va kāme purime va jappaɱ.|| ||

774. Kāmesu giddhā pasutā pamūḷhā||
Avadāniyā te visame niviṭṭhā,||
Dukkhūpanitā paridevayanti:||
"Kiɱ su bhavissāma ito cutāse."|| ||

775. Tasmā hi sikkhetha idh'eva jantu:||
Yaɱ kiñci jaññā 'visaman' ti loke,||
Na tassa hetu visamaɱ careyya,||
Appaɱ hi taɱ jīvitaɱ āhu dhīrā.|| ||

776. Passāmi loke pariphandamānaɱ||
Pajaɱ imaɱ taṇhāgataɱ bhavesu,||
Hinā narā maccumukhe lapanti||
Avitataṇhāse bhav-ā-bhavesu.|| ||

777. Mamāyite passatha phandamāne||
Macche va appodake khiṇasote,||
Etam pi disvā amamo careyya||
Bhavesu āsattim akubbamano.|| ||

778. Ubhosu antesu vineyya chandaɱ||
Phassaɱ pariññāya anānugiddho,||
Yad attagarahi, tad akubbamāno||
Na lippati diṭṭhasutesu dhīro.|| ||

[153] 779. Saññaɱ pariññā vitareyya oghaɱ||
Pariggahesu muni nōpalitto,||
Abbuḷhasallo caraɱ appamatto||
Nāsiɱsati lokam imaɱ parañ cā ti.|| ||

Guhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

3. Duṭṭhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

780. Vadanti ve duṭṭhamanā pi eke||
Atho pi ve saccamanā vadanti,||
Vādañ ca jātaɱ muni no upeti,||
Tasmā muni n'atthi khilo kuhiñci.|| ||

781. Sakaɱ hi diṭṭhiɱ katham accayeyya||
Chandānunito ruciyā niviṭṭho,||
Sayaɱ samatatāni pakubbamāno||
Yathā hi jāneyya, tathā vadeyya|| ||

782. Yo attano silavatāni jantu||
Anānupaṭṭho ca paresa pāvā,||
Anariyadhamamaɱ kusalā tam āhu,||
Yo ātumānaɱ sayam eva pāvā.|| ||

783. Santo ca bhikkhu abhinibabutatto||
"Iti'han" ti sīlesu akatthamāno,||
Tam ariya-Dhammaɱ kusalā vadanti,||
Yass'ussadā n'atthi kuhiñci loke|| ||

[154] 784. Pakapapitā saŋkhatā yassa dhammā||
Purakkhatā santi avivadātā,||
Yad attani passati ānisaɱsaɱ||
Taɱ nissito kuppapaṭiccasantiɱ|| ||

785. Diṭṭhinivesā na hi svātivattā||
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahitaɱ,||
Tasmā naro tesu nivesanesu||
Nirassati ādisati-cca dhammaɱ.|| ||

786. Dhonassa hi n'atthi kuhiñci loke||
Pakappitā diṭṭhi bhav-ā-bhavesu,||
Māyañ ca mānañ ca pahāya dhono||
Sa kena gaccheyya: anupayo so.|| ||

787. Upayo hi dhammesu upeti vādaɱ,||
anupayaɱ kena kathaɱ vadeyya,||
Attaɱ nirattaɱ na hi tassa atthi:||
Adhosi so diṭṭhi-m-idh'eva sabba ti.|| ||

Duṭṭhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

4. Suddhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

788. 'Passāmi suddhaɱ paramaɱ arogaɱ||
Diṭṭhena saɱsuddhi narassa hoti,||
Etābhijānaɱ 'paraman' ti ñatvā||
Suddhānupassī ti pacceti ñāṇaɱ|| ||

[155] 789. Diṭṭhena ce suddhi narassa hoti||
Ñāṇena vā so pajahāti dukkhaɱ,||
Aññena so sujjhati sopadhīko||
Diṭṭhi hi naɱ pāva tathā vadānaɱ.|| ||

790. Na brāhmaṇo aññato suddhim āha||
Diṭṭhe sute sīla-vate mute vā,||
Puññe ca pāpe ca anupalitto||
Attañajaho na-y-idha pakubbamāno.|| ||

791. Purimaɱ pahāya aparaɱ sitāse||
Ejānugā *te na* taranti Saŋghagaɱ,||
Te uggahāyanti nirassajanti||
Kapiva sākhaɱ pamuñcaɱ gahāya.|| ||

792. Sayaɱ samādayaɱ vatāni jantu||
Uccāvacaɱ gacchati saññasatto,||
vidvā ca vedehi samecca dhammaɱ||
Na uccāvacaɱ gacchati bhuripañño.|| ||

793. Sa sabba-dhammesu visenibhūto||
Yaɱ kiñci diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā,||
Tam evadassiɱ vivaṭaɱ carantaɱ||
Kenidha lokasmiɱ vikappayeyya.|| ||

794. Na kappayanti, na purekkharonti,||
"Accantasuddhī" ti na te vadanti,||
[156] Adāna-ganthaɱ gathitaɱ visajja||
Āsaɱ na kubbanti kuhiñci loke.|| ||

795. Simātigo brāhmaṇo tassa n'atthi||
Ñatvā va disvā va samuggahitaɱ,||
Na rāga-rāgi na virāga-ratto||
Tassidha n'atthi param uggahitan ti.|| ||

Suddhaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

5. Paramaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

796. 'Paraman' ti diṭṭhisu paribbasāno||
Yad utatariɱ kurute jantu loke,||
"Hinā" ti aññe tato sabba-m-āha:||
Tasmā vivādāni avitivatto.|| ||

797. Yad attani passati ānisaɱsaɱ||
Diṭṭhe sute sīla-vate mute vā,||
Tad eva so tattha samuggahāya||
Nihinato passati sabbam aññaɱ.|| ||

798. Taɱ vā pi ganthaɱ kusalā vadanti,||
Yaɱ nissito passati hinam aññaɱ,||
Tasmā hi diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā||
Sīlabbataɱ bhikkhu na nissayeyya.|| ||

[157] 799. Diṭṭhim pi lokasmiɱ na kappayeyya||
Ñāṇena vā sīla-vatena vā pi,||
'Samo' ti attānaɱ anupaneyya||
'Hino' na maññetha 'visasi' vā pi.|| ||

800. Attaɱ pahāya anupādiyāno||
Ñāṇe pi so nissayaɱ no karoti,||
Sa ve viyattesu na vaggasāri||
Diṭṭhim pi so na pacceti kiñci.|| ||

801. Yasasūbhayante paṇidhidha n'atthi||
Bhavābhavāya idha vā huraɱ vā,||
Nivesanā tassa na santi keci||
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaɱ.|| ||

802. Tassidha diṭṭhe va sute mute vā||
Pakappitā n'atthi aṇū pi saññā,||
Taɱ brāhmaṇaɱ diṭṭhim anādiyānaɱ||
Kenidha lokasmiɱ vikappayeyya.|| ||

803. Na kapapyanti na purekkharonti||
Dhammā pi tesaɱ na paṭicchitāse,||
[158] na brāhmaṇo sīla-vatena neyyo,||
Pāraɱgato na pacceti tādī ti.|| ||

Paramaṭṭhaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

6. Jarā Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

804. Appaɱ vata jīvitaɱ idaɱ||
Oraɱ vasassatā pi miyati,||
Yo ce pi aticca jīvati,||
Atha kho so jarasā pi miyati.|| ||

805. Socanti janā mamāyite,||
Na hi santā niccā pariggahā,||
Vinābhāvasantam ev'idaɱ||
Iti disvā nāgāram āvase.|| ||

806. Maraṇena pi taɱ pahīyati,||
Yaɱ puriso 'mama-y-idan' ti maññati,||
Evaɱ pi viditvā paṇḍito||
Na mamattāya nametha māmako.|| ||

807. Supinena yathā pi saŋgataɱ||
PaṭiBuddho puriso na passati,||
[159] Evam pi piyāyitaɱ janaɱ||
Petaɱ kāla-kataɱ na passati.|| ||

808. Diṭṭhā pi sutā pi te janā,||
Yesaɱ nāmam idaɱ pavuccati,||
Nāmam evāvasissati||
Akkheyyaɱ petassa janatuno.|| ||

809. Sokaparideva-maccharaɱ||
Na jahanti giddhā mamāyite,||
Tasmā munayo pariggahaɱ||
Hitvā acariɱsu khemadassino.|| ||

810. Patilinavarassa bhikkhuno||
Bhajamānassa vivittamānasaɱ,||
Sāmaggiyam āhu tassa taɱ||
Yo attānaɱ bhavane na dassaye.|| ||

811. Sabbattha muni anissito||
Na piyaɱ kubbati no pi appiyaɱ,||
Tasmiɱ paradeva-maccharaɱ||
Paṇṇe vāri yathā na lippati.|| ||

812. Udabindu yathā pi pokkhare||
Padume vāri yathā na lippati,||
Evaɱ muni nōpalippati||
Yad idaɱ diṭṭhasutaɱ mutesu vā|| ||

[160] 813. Dhono na hi tena maññati||
Yad idaɱ diṭṭhasutaɱ mutesu vā,||
Nā aññena visuddhim icchati:||
Na hi so rajjati no virajjati ti.|| ||

Jarā Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

7. Tissametteyya Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

814. "Methunam anuyuttassa icc'āyasmā Tisso Metteyyo||
Vighātaɱ brūhi mārisa,||
Sutvāna tava sāsanaɱ viveke sikkhissāmase."|| ||

815. "Methunam anuyuttassa Metteyyā ti Bhagavā||
Mussat'evā pi sāsanaɱ,||
Micchā ca paṭipajjati, etaɱ tasmiɱ anāriyaɱ.|| ||

816. Eko pubbe caritvāna methunaɱ yo nisevati,||
Yāniɱ bhantaɱ va taɱ loke hinam āhu puthujjanaɱ.|| ||

817. Yaso kittiñ ca yā pubbe, hāyat'evā pi tassa sā,||
Etam pi disvā sikkhetha methunaɱ vippahātave.|| ||

818. Saɱkappehi pareto so kapaṇo viya jhāyati,||
Sutvā paresaɱ nigghosaɱ maŋku hoti tathāvidho.|| ||

819. Atha Satthāni kurute paravādehi codito,||
Esa khav'assa māhāgedho: mosavajjaɱ pagāhati.|| ||

820. Paṇḍito ti samaññāto ekacariyaɱ adhiṭṭhito,||
Athā pi methune yutto mando va parikissati.|| ||

[161] 821. Etam ādinavaɱ ñatvā muni pubbāpare idha,||
Ekacariyaɱ daḷhaɱ kayirā, na nisevetha methunaɱ|| ||

822. Vivekaɱ yeva sikkhetha, *etad ariyānam* uttamaɱ,||
Tena seṭṭho na maññetha, sa ve Nibbānasantake.|| ||

823. Rittassa munino carato kāmesu anapekkhino||
Oghatiṇṇassa pihayanti kāmesu gathitā pajā" ti.|| ||

Tissameteyya Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

8. Pasūra Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

824. "Idh'eva suddhi" iti vādiyanti,||
Nāññesu dhammesu visuddhim āhu,||
Yaɱ nissitā, tattha subhaɱ vadānā||
Paccekasaccesu puthu niviṭṭhā.|| ||

825. Te vādakāmā parisaɱ vigayha||
Bālaɱ dahanti mithu añña-maññaɱ,||
Vadanti te aññasitā kathojjaɱ||
Pasaɱsakāmā kusalā vadānā.|| ||

826. Yutto kathāyaɱ parisāya majjhe||
Pasaɱsam icchaɱ vinighāti hoti,||
Apāhatasmiɱ pana maŋku hoti,||
Nindāya so kuppati randhamesī.|| ||

[162] 827. Yam assa vādaɱ parihinam āhu||
Apāhataɱ pañahavimaɱsakāse,||
Paridevati socati hinavādo,||
'Upaccagā man' ti anutthuṇāti.|| ||

828. Ete vivādā samaṇesu jātā||
Etesu ugaghāti nighāti hoti,||
Etam pi disvā virame kathojjaɱ||
Na h'aññadatth'atthi pasaɱsalāhā.|| ||

829. Pasaɱsito vā pana tattha hoti||
Akkhāya vādaɱ parisāya majjhe,||
So hassati uṇṇamati-cca tena||
Pappuyya tam atthaɱ yathā mano ahu.|| ||

830. Yā uṇṇati, sāssa vighātabhūmi,||
Mānātimānaɱ vadate pan'eso,||
*Etam pi disvā na vivādayetha,*||
Na hi tena suddhiɱ kusalā vadanti.|| ||

831. Suro yathā rājakhādāya puṭṭho||
Abhigajjam eti paṭisuram icchaɱ,||
Yen'eva so tena palehi sūra,||
Pubbe va n'atthi yad idaɱ yudhāya.|| ||

832. Ye diṭṭhim uggayha vivādayanti||
"Idam eva saccan" ti ca vādayanti,||
[163] Te tvaɱ vadassu, na hi te'dha atthi||
Vādamhi jāte paṭisenikattā.|| ||

833. Visenikatvā pana ye caranti||
Diṭṭhihi diṭṭhiɱ avirujjhamānā,||
Tesu tvaɱ kiɱ labhetho PAsura,||
Yes'idha n'atthi param uggahitaɱ.|| ||

834. Atha tvaɱ pavitakkam āgamā||
Manasā diṭṭhi-gatāni cintayanto,||
Dhonena yugaɱ samāgamā,||
Na hi tvaɱ sagghasi sampayātave ti.|| ||

PAsura Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

9. Māgandiya Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

835. "Disvāna Taṇhaɱ *Aratiɱ Ragañ cā*||
Nāhosi chando api methunasmiɱ,||
Kim ev'idaɱ muttakarisapuṇṇaɱ,||
Pādā pi naɱ samaphusituɱ na icchi."|| ||

[164] 836. "Etādisaɱ ce ratanaɱ na icchasi||
Nāriɱ narindehi bahūhi patthitaɱ,||
Diṭṭhiggataɱ sīla-vatānujīvitaɱ||
Bhavūpapattiñ ca vadesi kidisaɱ."|| ||

837. "'Idaɱ vadāmi' ti na tassa hoti Māgandiyā ti Bhagavā||
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahitaɱ,||
Passañ ca diṭṭhisu anuggahāya||
Ajjhattasantiɱ pacinaɱ adassaɱ."|| ||

838. "Vinicchayā yāni pakappitāni, iti Māgandiyo||
Te ve muni brūsi anuggahāya,||
'Ajjhantasanti' ti yam etam atthaɱ.||
Kathaɱ nu dhirehi paveditaɱ taɱ."|| ||

839. "Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena Māgandiyā ti Bhagavā||
Sīlabbatenā pi *na suddhim* āha,||
Adiṭṭhiyā asasutiyā añṇāṇā||
Asīlatā abbatā no pi tena||
Ete ca nissajja anuggahāya||
Santo anissāya bhavaɱ na jappe."|| ||

840. "No ce kira diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena iti Māgandiyo||
Sīlabbatenā pi visudadhim āha||
[165] Adiṭṭhiyā assutiyā añṇāṇā,||
Asīlatā abbatā no pi tena,||
