Maññe-m-ahaɱ momuham eva dhammaɱ||
Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiɱ."|| ||

841. "Diṭṭhiñ ca nissāya anupucchamāno Māgandiyā ti Bhagavā||
Samuggahitesu pamoham āgā||
Ito ca nāddakkhi aṇum pi saññaɱ||
Tasma tuvaɱ momuhato dahāsi.|| ||

842. Samo vihesi uda cā nibhino||
Yo maññati so vivadetha tena,||
Tisu vidhāsu avikampamāno—||
'Samo visesi' ti na tassa hoti.|| ||

843. 'Saccan' ti so brāhmaṇo kiɱ vadeyya,||
'Musā' ti vā so vivadetha kena:||
Yasmiɱ samaɱ visamaɱ cāpi n'atthi||
Sa kena vādaɱ paṭisaɱyujeyya|| ||

844. Okam pahāya aniketasāri||
Gāme akubabaɱ muni santhavāni,||
Kāmehi ritto apurekkharāno||
Kathaɱ na viggayha janena kayirā.|| ||

845. Ye hi vivitto vicareyya loke,||
Na tāni uggayha vadeyya nāgo,||
[166] elamabujaɱ kaṇṭakaɱ vārijaɱ yathā||
Jalena paŋkena c'anūpalittaɱ,||
Evaɱ muni santivādo agiddho||
Kāme ca loke ca anupalitto.|| ||

846. Na vedagu diṭṭhiyā na mutiyā||
Sa mānam eti, na hi tammayo so,||
Na kamamanā no pi sutena neyyo||
Anupanito sa nivesanesu.|| ||

847. Saññāvirattassa na santi gatthā||
Paññāvimuttassa na satti mohā,||
Saññañ ca diṭṭiñ ca ye aggahesuɱ||
Te ghaṭṭayantā- vicaranti loke" ti.|| ||

Māgandiya Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

10. Purābheda Sutta (Suribheda Suttaɱ)

[faus] [than]

 

848. "'Kathaɱdassi kathaɱsilo upasanto' ti vuccati,||
Taɱ me Gotama pabrūhi pucchito uttamaɱ naraɱ."|| ||

849. "Vitataṇho purā bhedā||
iti Bhagavā||
pubbam antam anissito,||
Vemajjhe nūpasaŋkheyyo, tassa n'atthi purekkhataɱ.|| ||

[167] 850. Akkodhano asantāsi, avikatthi akukkuco,||
Mantabhāṇi anuddhato, sa ve vācāyato muni.|| ||

851. Nirāsatti anāgate atitaɱ nānusocati,||
Vivekadassi phassesu diṭṭhisu ca na niyati,|| ||

852. Patilino akuhako, apihālu amaccharī,||
Appagabbho ajeguccho, pesuṇeyye ca no yuto.|| ||

853. Sātiyesu anassāvi ati-māne ca no yuto,||
Saṇho ca paṭibhānavā, na saddo na virajjati.|| ||

854. Lābhakamyā na sikkhati, alābhe na ca kuppati,||
Aviruddho ca taṇhāya rase ca nānugijjhati.|| ||

855. Upekkhako sadā sato na loke maññate samaɱ,||
Na visesi na nīceyyo, tassa no santi ussadā.|| ||

856. Yassa nissayatā n'atthi ñatvā dhammaɱ anissito,||
Bhavāya vibhavāya vā taṇhā yassa na vijjati.|| ||

857. Taɱ brūmi upasanto ti kāmesu anapekkhinaɱ,||
Ganthā tassa na vijjanti, atāri so visattikaɱ.|| ||

858. Na tassa puttā pasavo vā khettaɱ vatthuɱ na vijjati||
[168] Antāɱ vā pi nirattāɱ vā na tasmiɱ upalabbhati.|| ||

859. Yena naɱ vajju puthujjanā atho samaṇa-brāhmaṇā,||
Taɱ tassa apurekkhatāɱ, tasmā vādesu n'ejati.|| ||

860. Vitagedho amacchari na ussesu vadate muni,||
Na samesu na omesu, kappaɱ n'eti akappiyo.|| ||

861. Yassa loke sakaɱ n'atthi, asatā ca na socati,||
Dhammesu ca na gacchiti, sa ve santo ti vuccati" ti.|| ||

Purābheda Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

11. Kalahavivadā Sutta (Nalahavivāda Suttaɱ)

[faus] [than]

 

862. "Kuto pahūtā kalahā vivādā||
Paridevasokā sahamacchirā ca,||
Mānātimānā sahapesunā ca,||
Kuto pahūtā te, tad iŋgha brūhi."|| ||

863. "Piyā pahūtā kalahā vivādā||
Paridevasokā samaccharā ca,||
Mānātimānā sahapesunā ca,||
Macchiriyayuttā kalahā vivādā||
Vivādajātesu ca pesunāni."|| ||

[169] 864. "Piyā su lokasmaɱ kutonidānā ye vā pi lobhā vicaranti loke,||
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca kutonidānā,||
Ye samparāyāya narassa honti."|| ||

865. "Chandanidānāni piyāni loke||
Ye vā pi lobhā vicaranti loke,||
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca itonidānā,||
Ye samparāyāya narassa honti."|| ||

866. "Chando nu lokasmiɱ kutonidāno,||
Vinicchāyā vā pi kuto pahūtā,||
Kodho mosavajjañ ca kathaɱ-kathaɱ ca||
Ye vā pi dhammā samaṇena vuttā."|| ||

867. "'Sātaɱ asātan' ti yam āhu loke,||
Tam ūpanissāya pahoti chando,||
Rūpesu disvā vibhavaɱ bhavañ ca||
Vinicchayaɱ kurute janatu loke.|| ||

868. Kodho mosavajjañ ca kathaɱ-kathaɱ ca||
Ete pi dhamamā dvaya-m-eva sante:||
Kathaɱkathī ñāṇapathāya sikkhe,||
Ñatvā pavuttā samaṇena dhammā."|| ||

869. "Sātaɱ asātañ ca kutonidānā,||
Kismiɱ asante na bhavanti h'ete,||
'Vibhavaɱ bhavañ cāpi' yam etam atthaɱ,||
Etaɱ me pabrūhi yatonidānaɱ."|| ||

870. "Phassānidānaɱ sātaɱ asātaɱ||
Phasse asante na bhavanti h'ete,||
[170] 'Vibhavaɱ bhavañ cāpi' yam etam atthaɱ||
Etaɱ te pabrūmi itonidānaɱ."|| ||

871. "Phasso nu lokasmiɱ kutonidāno,||
Pariggahā vā pi kuto pahūtā,||
Kismiɱ asante na mamattam atthi,||
Kismiɱ vibhute na phusanti phassā."|| ||

872. "Nāmañ ca rūpañ ca paṭicca phassā||
Icchānidānāni pariggahāni,||
Icchā na santyā na mamattam atthi,||
Rūpe vibhute na phusanti phassā."|| ||

873. "Kathaɱ-sametassa vibhoti rūpaɱ,||
Sukhaɱ dukhaɱ vā pi kathaɱ vibhoti,||
Etaɱ me pabrūhi yathā vibhoti,||
'Taɱ jāniyāma' iti me mano ahū."|| ||

874. "Na saññasaññi na visaññasaññi||
No pi asaññi na vibhūtasaññi,||
Evaɱ-sametassa vibhoti rūpaɱ,||
Saññānidānā hi papañcasaŋkhā."|| ||

875. "Yaɱ taɱ apucchimha akittayi no,||
Aññaɱ taɱ pucchāma, tad iŋgha brūhi,||
[171] Ettāvat'aggaɱ no vadanti h'eke||
Yakkhassa suddhiɱ idha paṇḍitāse,||
Udāhu aññam pi vadanti etto."|| ||

876. "Ettāvavat'aggam pi vadanti h'eke||
Yakkhassa suddhiɱ idha paṇḍitāse,||
Tesaɱ pun'eke samayaɱ vadanti||
Anupādisese kusalā vadānā.|| ||

877. Ete ca ñatvā 'upanissitā' ti||
Ñatvā muni nissaye so vimaɱsī,||
Ñatvā vimutto na vimādam eti||
Bhavābhavāya na sameti dhīro" ti.|| ||

Kalahavivāda Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

12. Cūlaviyūha Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

878. "Sakaɱ sakaɱ diṭṭhi paribbasānā||
Viggayha nānā kusalā vadanti:||
'Yo evaɱ jānāti, sa vedi dhammaɱ||
Idaɱ paṭikkosam akevali so.'|| ||

879. Evam pi viggayha vivādiyanati,||
'Bālo paro akakusalo' ti cāhu||
Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaɱ||
Sabbe va h'ime kusalā vadānā."|| ||

[172] 880. "Parassa ce dhammam anānujānaɱ||
Bālo mago hoti nihīnapañño,||
Sabbe va bālā sunihīnapaññā||
Sabbe v'ime diṭṭhi paribbasānā.|| ||

881. Sandiṭṭhiyā ce pana vīvadātā||
Saɱsuddhapaññā kusalā mutimā,||
na tesaɱ koci parihīnapañño||
Diṭṭhi hi tesam pi tathā samattā.|| ||

882. Na vāham 'etaɱ tathiyan' ti brūmi,||
Yam āhu bālā mithu añña-maññaɱ,||
Sakaɱ sakaɱ diṭṭhim akaɱsu saccaɱ||
Tasmā hi 'bālo' ti paraɱ dahanti."|| ||

883. "Yam āhu 'saccaɱ tathiyan' ti eke,||
Tam āhu aññe 'tucchaɱ musā' ti,||
Evam pi viggayha vivādiyanti,||
kasmā na ekaɱ samaṇā vadanti."|| ||

884. "Ekaɱ hi saccaɱ na dutiyam atthi,||
Yasmiɱ pajāno vivade pajānaɱ,||
Nāna te saccāni sayaɱ thunanti,||
Tasmā na ekaɱ samaṇā vadanti."|| ||

[173] 885. "Kasmā nu saccāni vadanti nānā||
Pavādiyāse kusalā vadānā:||
Saccāni su tāni bahuni nānā||
Udāhu te takkam anussaranti."|| ||

886. "Na h'eva saccāni bahūni nānā,||
Aññatra saññāya niccāni loke,||
Takkañ ca diṭṭhīsu pakappayitvā||
'Saccaɱ, musā' ti dvaya-dhammam āhu.|| ||

887. Diṭṭhe sute sīla-vate mute vā||
Ete ca nissāya vimānadassi,||
Vinicchaye ṭhatvā pahassamāno||
'Bālo paro akakusalo' ti cāha.|| ||

888. Yen'eva 'bālo' ti paraɱ dahāti,||
Tenātumānaɱ 'kusalo' ti cāha,||
Sayam attanā so kusalo vadāno||
Aññaɱ vimāneti, tath'eva pāvā|| ||

889. Atīsāradiṭṭhiyā so samanto||
Mānena matto paripuṇṇamāni,||
Sayam eva sāmaɱ manasābhisitto||
Diṭṭhi hi sā tassa tathā samattā.|| ||

890. Parassa ce hi vacasā nihino||
Tumo sahā hoti nihinapañño,||
Atha ce sayaɱ vedagu hoti dhīro||
Na koci bālo samaṇesu atthi.|| ||

[174] 891. 'Aññaɱ ito yābhivadanti dhammaɱ||
Aparaddhā sudadhim akevalīno,||
Evam hi tithyā puthuso vadanti,||
Sandiṭṭhirāgena *hi te* 'bhirattā|| ||

892. 'Idh'eva suddhi iti vādiyanti,||
Nāññesu dhammesu visuddham āhu,||
Evam pi tithyā puthuso niviṭṭhā||
Sakāyane tattha daḷhaɱ vadānā.|| ||

893. Sakāyane cāpi daḷhaɱ vadāno||
Kam ettha 'bālo' ti paraɱ daheyya,||
Sayam eva so medhakaɱ āvaheyya||
Paraɱ vadaɱ bālam asuddhidhammaɱ.|| ||

894. Vinicchaye ṭhatvā sayaɱ pamāya||
Uddhaɱ so lokasmiɱ vivādam eti,||
Hitvāna sabbāni vinicchayāni||
Na medhakaɱ kurute janatu loke" ti.|| ||

Cuḷaviyuha Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

13. Mahāviyūha Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

895. "Ye kec'ime diṭṭhi paribbasānā||
'Idam eva saccan' ti vivādayanti,||
Sabbe va te nindam anvānayanti||
Atho pasaɱsam pi labhanti tattha."|| ||

[175] 896. "Appaɱ hi etaɱ na alaɱ samāya,||
Duve vivādassa phalāni brūmi,||
Etam pi disvā na vivādayetha||
Khemābhipassaɱ avivādabhumiɱ.|| ||

897. Yā kāc'imā sammutiyo puthujjā||
Sabbā va etā na upeti vidvā,||
Anupayo so upayaɱ kim eyya||
Diṭṭhe sute khantim akubbamāno.|| ||

898. Siluttamā saññamenāhu sudadhiɱ||
Vataɱ samādāya upaṭṭhitāse,||
'Idh'eva sikkhema, ath'assa suddhiɱ'||
Bhavūpanītā kusalā vadānā.|| ||

899. Sace cuto silavatato hoti||
Sa vedhati kammaɱ virādhayitvā,||
Sa jappati paṭṭhayatidha sudadhiɱ||
Satthā va hīno pavasaɱ gharamhā.|| ||

900. Sīlabbataɱ vā pi pahāya sabbaɱ||
Kammañ ca sāvajjanavajjam etaɱ,||
[176] 'Suddhi, asudadhī' ti apatthayāno||
Virato care santim anuggahāya.|| ||

901. Tapūpanissāya jigucchitaɱ vā||
Atha vā pi diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā,||
Uddhaɱsarā suddhim anutthuṇanti||
Avitataṇhāse bhav-ā-bhavesu.|| ||

902. Patthayamānassa hi jappitāni||
Saɱvedhitaɱ cāpi pakappitesu:||
Cutūpapāto idha yassa n'atthi||
Sa kena vedheyya kuhiñ ca jappe.|| ||

903. "Yam āhu dhammaɱ 'paraman' ti eke||
Tam eva 'hinan' ti panāhu aññe,||
Sacco nu vādo katamo imesāɱ||
Sabbe va hīme kusalā vadānā.|| ||

904. Sakaɱ hi dhammaɱ paripuṇṇam āhu||
*Aññassa dhammaɱ pana hīnam āhu,*||
Evam pi viggayha vivādiyanti||
Sakaɱ sakaɱ samamutim āhu saccaɱ."|| ||

905. "Parassa ce vambhayitena hīno||
Na koci dhammesu visesi assa,||
Puthū hi aññassa vadanti dhammaɱ||
Nihinato samahi daḷhaɱ vadānā|| ||

[177] 906. Sadhammapūjā ca panā tath'eva||
Yathā pasaɱ-santi sakāyanāni,||
Sabbe va vādā tathivā bhaveyyuɱ||
Sudhi hi n'esaɱ paccattam eva.|| ||

907. Na brāhmaṇassa paraneyyam atthi||
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaɱ,||
Tasmā vivādāni upātivatto||
Na hi seṭṭhato passati dhammam aññaɱ.|| ||

908. 'Jānāmi passāmi, tath'eva etaɱ'||
Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiɱ||
Addakkhi ce, kim hi tumassa tena||
Atisitvā aññena vadanti suddhiɱ.|| ||

909. Passaɱ naro dakkhiti nāma-rūpaɱ||
Disvāna vāññassati tāni-m-eva:||
Kāmaɱ bahuɱ passatu appakaɱ vā||
Na hi tena suddhiɱ kusalā vadanti|| ||

910. Nivissavādi na hi suddināyo||
Pakappitaɱ daṭṭhi purekkharāno,||
Yaɱ nissito, tattha subhaɱ vadāno,||
Suddhiɱvado tattha tath'addasā so.|| ||

911. Na brāhmaṇo kappam upeti saŋkhaɱ||
Na diṭṭhisāri na pi ñāṇabandhu||
[178] Ñatvā ca so sammutiyo puthujjā||
Upekkhati, uggahaṇanta-m-aññe|| ||

912. Visajja ganthāni munidha loke||
Vivādajātesu na vaggasārī,||
Satto asantesu upekkhako so||
Anuggaho, uggahaṇta-m-aññe|| ||

913. Pubbāsave hitvā nave akubbaɱ||
Na chandagū no pi nivissavādo,||
Sa vippamutto diṭṭhigatehi dhīro||
Na lippati loke anattagarahī.|| ||

914. Sa sabba-dhammesu visenibhūto,||
Yaɱ kiñci diṭṭhiɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā,||
Sa pannabhāro muni vipapayutto||
Na kappiyo nuparato na patthiyo" ti.|| ||

Mahāviyuha Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

14. Tuvaṭaka Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

[179] 915. "Pucchāmi taɱ Ādiccabandhuɱ||
Vicekaɱ santipadañ ca mahesiɱ,||
Kathaɱ disvā nibbāti bhikkhu||
Anupādiyāno lokasmiɱ kiñci."|| ||

916. "Mūlaɱ papañ ca saŋkhāya iti Bhagavā||
'Mantā asmi' ti sabbam uparundhe,||
Yā kāci taṇhā ajjhattaɱ||
Tāsaɱ vinayā sadā sato sikkhe.|| ||

917. Yaɱ kiñci dhammam abhijaññā,||
Ajjhattaɱ atha vā pi bahiddhā,||
Na tena thāmaɱ kubbetha||
Na hi sā nibbuti sataɱ vuttā:|| ||

918. Seyyo na tena maññeyya||
Niceyyo atha vā pi sarikkho,||
Phuṭṭho anekarūpehi||
Nātumānaɱ vikappayaɱ tiṭṭhe|| ||

919. Ajjhattam eva upasame,||
Nāññato bhikkhu santim eseyya:||
Ajjhattaɱ upasantassa||
n'atthi attā, kuto nirattā vā.|| ||

[180] 920. Majjhe yathā samuddassa||
Ūmi no jāyati, ṭhito hoti,||
Evaɱ ṭhito anej'assa:||
Ussadaɱ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci."|| ||

921. "Akittayi vivaṭacakkhu||
Sakkhi dhammaɱ parissayavinayaɱ.||
Paṭipadaɱ vadehi, bhaddan te,||
Pātimokkhaɱ atha vā pi samādhiɱ."|| ||

922. "Cakkhuhi n'eva lol'assa,||
Gāmakathāya āvareyya sotaɱ,||
Rase ca nānugijjheyya||
Na ca mamāyetha kiñci lokasmiɱ.|| ||

923. Phassena yadā phuṭṭh'assa,||
Paridevaɱ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci||
Bhavaɱ ca nabhijappeyya||
Bheravesu ca na sampavedheyya.|| ||

924. Annānam atho pānānaɱ||
Khādaniyānaɱ atho pi vatthānaɱ,||
Laddhā na sannidhiɱ kayirā||
Na ca parittase tāni alabhamāno.|| ||

925. Jhāyī na pādalol'assa||
Virame kukkuccaɱ na-ppamajjeyya,||
Atha āsanesu sayanesu||
Appasaddesu bhikkhu vihareyya.|| ||

[181] 926. Niddaɱ na bahulī-kareyya,||
Jāgariyaɱ bhajeyya ātāpi,||
Tandiɱ māyaɱ hassaɱ khiḍḍaɱ||
Methunaɱ vippajahe savibhūsaɱ.|| ||

927. Āthabbaṇaɱ supinaɱ lakkhaṇaɱ||
No vidahe atho pi nakkhattaɱ,||
Virutañ ca gabbhakaraṇaɱ||
Tikicchaɱ māmako na seveyya|| ||

928. Nindāya na-ppavedheyya||
Na uṇṇameyya pasaɱsito bhikkhu,||
Lobhaɱ saha macchariyena||
Kodhaɱ pesuniyañ ca panudeyya.|| ||

929. Kayavikkaye na tiṭṭheyya,||
Upavādaɱ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci,||
Gāme ca nābhisajjeyya,||
Lābhakamyā janaɱ na lāpayeyya.|| ||

930. Na ca katthikā siyā bhikkhu||
Na ca vācaɱ payutaɱ bhāseyya,||
Pāgabbhiyaɱ na sikkheyya||
Kathaɱ viggāhikaɱ na kathayeyya.|| ||

931. Mosavajje na niyyetha,||
Sampajāno saṭhāni na kayirā,||
[182] Atha jivitena paññāya||
Sīla-vatena nāññam atimaññe.|| ||

932. Sutvā rusito bahuɱ vācaɱ||
Samaṇānaɱ puthuvacanānaɱ,||
Pharusena ne na paṭivajjā||
Na hi santo paṭisenikaronti.|| ||

933. Etañ ca dhammam aññāya||
Vicinaɱ bhikkhu sadā sato sikkhe,||
'Santi' ti nibbutiɱ ñatvā||
Sāsane Gotamassa na-ppamajjeyya.|| ||

934. Abhibhū hi so anabhibhūto||
Sakkhi dhammaɱ anītiham adassī,||
Tasmā hi tassa Bhagavato||
sāsane appamatto sadā namassam anusikkhe"||
ti Bhagavā ti.|| ||

Tuvaṭaka Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

15. Attadaṇḍa Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

935. "Attadaṇḍā bhayaɱ jātaɱ, janaɱ passatha medhakaɱ||
Saɱvegaɱ kittayissāmi yathā saɱvijitaɱ mayā.|| ||

[183] 936. Phandamānaɱ pajaɱ disvā macche appodake yatha,||
Aññamaññehi vyāruddhe disvā maɱ bhayam āvisi.|| ||

937. Samantaɱ asāro loko, disā sabbā sameritā,||
Icchāɱ bhavanam attano nāddasāsiɱ anositaɱ.|| ||

938. Osāne tv-eva vyāruddhe disvā me arati ahu,||
Ath'ettha sallaɱ addakkhiɱ duddasaɱ hadayanissitaɱ.|| ||

939. Yena sallena otiṇṇo disā sabbā vidhāvati,||
Tam eva sallaɱ ababuyha na dhāvati, nisidati.|| ||

940. Tattha sikkhānugīyanti||
Yāni loke gathitāni, na tesu pasuto siyā,||
Nibbijjha sabbasā kāme sikkhe Nibbānam attano.|| ||

941. Sacco siyā appagabbho amāyo rittapesuno,||
Akkodhano, lobhapāpaɱ vevicchaɱ vitare muni.|| ||

942. Niddaɱ tandiɱ sahe thinaɱ, pamādena na saɱvase,||
Atimāne na tiṭṭheyya Nibbānamanaso naro.|| ||

[184] 943. Mosavajje na niyyetha, rūpe snehaɱ na kubbaye,||
Mānañ ca parijāneyya, sahasā virato care.|| ||

944. Purāṇaɱ nābhinandeyya, nave khantiɱ na kubbaye,||
Hīyamāne na soceyya, ākāsaɱ na sito siyā.|| ||

945. Gedhaɱ brūmi "mahogho" ti ājavaɱ brūmi jappanaɱ,||
Ārammaṇaɱ pakappanaɱ, kāmapaŋko duraccayo.|| ||

946. Saccā avokkamma muni thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo,||
Sabbaɱ so paṭinissajja sa ve santo ti vuccati.|| ||

947. Sa ve vidvā, sa vedagū, ñatvā dhammaɱ anissito,||
Sammā so loke iriyāno na pihetī'dha kassaci.|| ||

948. Yo'dha kāme accatari saŋgaɱ loke duraccayaɱ,||
Na so socati nājjheti chinnasoto abandhano.|| ||

949. Yaɱ pubbe, taɱ visosehi, pacchā te māhu kiñcanaɱ,||
Majjhe ce no gahessasi, upasanto carissasi.|| ||

950. Sabbaso nāma-rūpasmiɱ yassa n'atthi mamāyitaɱ,||
Asatā ca socati, sa ve loke na jiyyati.|| ||

951. Yassa n'atthi 'idaɱ me' ti 'paresaɱ' vā pi kiñcanaɱ,||
Mamattaɱ so asaɱvindaɱ 'n'atthi me' ti na socati.|| ||

[185] 952. Aniṭṭhuri ananugiddho anejo sabbadhi samo,||
Tam ānisaɱsaɱ pabrūmi pucchito avikampinaɱ.|| ||

953. Anejassa vijānato n'atthi kācini saŋkhiti,||
Virato so viyārambā khemaɱ passati sabbadhi.|| ||

954. Na samesu na omesu na ussesu vadate muni,||
Santo so vitamacchero nādeti na nirassatī"||
ti Bhagavā ti.|| ||

Attadaṇḍa Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

16. Sāriputta Suttaɱ

[faus] [than]

 

955. "Na me diṭṭo ito pubbe||
Na-ssuto uda kassa ci,||
Icc'āyasmā Sāriputto||
Evaɱ vagguvado Satthā Tusitā gaṇi-m-āgato.|| ||

956. Sadevakassa lokassa, yathā dissati cakkhumā:||
Sabbaɱ tamaɱ vinodetvā eko va ratim ajjhagā.|| ||

[186] 957. Taɱ Buddhaɱ asitaɱ tādiɱ akuhaŋ gaṇim āgataɱ,||
Bahunnam idha baddhānaɱ atthi pañhena āgamaɱ.|| ||

958. Bhikkhuno vijigucchato bhajato rittam āsanaɱ,||
Rukkha-mūlaɱ susānaɱ vā, pabbatānaɱ guhāsu vā.|| ||

959. Uccāvacesu sayanesu, kivanto tattha bheravā,||
Ye hi bhikkhu na vedheyya nigghose sayanāsane.|| ||

960. Kati parissayā loke gacchato amataɱ disaɱ,||
Ye bhikkhu abhisambhave pantambhi sayanāsane.|| ||

961. Ky-āssa vyappathayo assu, ky-āss'assu idha gocarā,||
Kāni sīlabbatān'assu pahit'attassa bhikkhuno.|| ||

962. Kaɱ so sikkhaɱ samādāya ekodi nipako sato,||
Kammāro rajatass'eva niddhame malam attano."|| ||

963. "Vijiguccha-mānassa yad idaɱ phāsu||
Sāriputtā ti Bhagavā||
Rittāsanaɱ sayanaɱ sevato ce,||
Sambodhikāmassa, yathānudhammaɱ||
Taɱ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaɱ.|| ||

964. Pañcannaɱ dhīro bhayānaɱ na bhāye||
Bhikkhu sato (sa) pariyantacārī,||
Ḍaɱsādhipātānaɱ siriɱsapānaɱ||
Manussaphassānaɱ catu-p-padānaɱ.|| ||

[187] 965. Paradhammikānam pi na santaseyya||
Disvā pi tesaɱ bahuheravāni,||
Athāparāni abhisambhaveyya||
Parissayāni kusalānuesī.|| ||

966. Ātaŋkaphassena khudāya phuṭṭho||
Sītaɱ accuṇhaɱ adhivāsayeyya,||
So tehi phuṭṭho bahudhā anoko||
Viriyaɱ parakkamma daḷhaɱ kareyya.|| ||

967. Theyyaɱ na kareyya na musā bhaṇeyya,||
Mettāya phasse tasathāvarāni,||
Yad āvilattaɱ manaso vijaññā||
'Kaṇhassa pakkho' ti vinodayeyya.|| ||

968. Kodhātimānassa vasaɱ na gacche||
Mūlam pi tesaɱ palikhañña tiṭṭhe,||
Atha-ppiyaɱ vā pana appiyaɱ vā||
Addhā bhavanto abhisambhaveyya.|| ||

969. Paññaɱ purakkhatvā kalyāṇapī ti||
Vikkhambheyya tāni parissayāni,||
Aratiɱ sabhetha sayanamhi pante||
Caturo sahetha paridevadhamme.|| ||

970. 'Kiɱ su asissāmi, kuvaɱ vā asissaɱ||
Dukkhaɱ vata settha, kuv'ajja sessaɱ,'||
Ete vitakke paridevaneyye||
Vinayetha sekho aniketasāri.|| ||

[188] 971. Annañ ca laddhā vasanañ ca kāle||
Mattaɱ so jaññā idha tosanatthaɱ,||
Sotesu gutto yatacāri gāme||
Rusito pi vācaɱ pharusaɱ na vajjā.|| ||

972. Okkhitta-cakkhu na ca pādalolo||
Jhānānuyutto bahujāgar'assa,||
Upekham ārabbha samāhitatto||
Takkāsayaɱ kukkucciy'upacchinde.|| ||

973. Cudito vacīhi satimābhinande||
Sabrahma-cārisu khilaɱ pabhinde,||
Vācaɱ pamuñce kusalaɱ nātivelaɱ||
Janavādadhammāya na cetayeyya.|| ||

974. Athāparaɱ pañca rajāni loke||
Yesaɱ satimā vinayāya sikkhe:||
Rūpesu saddesu atho rasesu||
Gandhesu phassesu sahetha rāgaɱ.|| ||

975. Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaɱ||
Bhikkhu satimā su-vimutta-citto,||
[189] Kālena so sammā dhammaɱ parivimaɱsamāno||
Ekodibhūto vihane tamaɱ so"||
ti Bhagavā ti.|| ||

Sāriputta Suttaɱ Niṭṭhitaɱ.|| ||

Aṭṭhakavaggo catuttho.|| ||

Tassuddānaɱ: -||
Kāma-Guhaṭṭha Duṭṭhāva Suddhaṭṭha Paramā jarā,||
Metteyyo ca Pasuro ca Māgandi Purābhedanaɱ.||
Kalahaɱ dve va Vyuhāni punar eva Tuvaṭṭakaɱ||
Attadaṇḍavara Suttaɱ Therapañehana soḷasa,||
Tāni etāni suttāni Aṭṭhakavaggikā ti.|| ||

 

[190]

V. Pārāyana Vagga

 

 

1. Vatthugāthā

[faus]|| ||

 

976. Kosalānaɱ purā rammā āgamā Dakkhiṇāpathaɱ,||
Ākiñcaññaɱ patthayāno brāhmaṇo mantapāragu.|| ||

977. So Assakassa visaye Aḷakassa samāsane,||
Vasi Godhāvarikule uñchena ca phalena ca.|| ||

978. Tass'eva upanissāya gāmo ca vipulo ahū,||
Tato jātena āyena mahāyaññama kappayi.|| ||

979. Mahāyaññaɱ yajitvāna puna pāvisi assamaɱ,||
Tasmiɱ pati paviṭṭhamhi añño āgañchi brāhmaṇo.|| ||

980. Ugghaṭṭapādo tasito paɱkadanto rajassiro,||
So ca naɱ upasankamma satāni pañca yā cati.|| ||

981. Tam enaɱ Bāvarī disvā āsanena nimantayi,||
Sukhañ ca kusalaɱ pucchi, idaɱ vacanam abravi.|| ||

982. "Yaɱ kho mamaɱ deyya-dhammaɱ sabbaɱ vissajjitaɱ mayā,||
Anujānāhi me brahme, n'atthi pañca satāni me."|| ||

[191] 983. "Sace me yā camānassa bhavaɱ nānupadassati,||
Sattame divase tuyhaɱ muddhā phalatu sattadhā.|| ||

984. Abhisankharitvā kuhako bheravaɱ so akittayi,||
Tassa taɱ vacanaɱ sutvā Bāvarī dukkhito ahū.|| ||

985. Ussussati an-āhāro soka-sallasamappito,||
Atho pi evaɱ cittassa jhāne na ramatī mano.|| ||

986. Utrastaɱ dukkhitaɱ disvā devatā atthakāminī,||
Bāvariɱ upasankamma idaɱ vacanam abravi.|| ||

987. "Na so muddhaɱ pajānāti kuhako so dhan'atthiko,||
Muddhani muddhapāte vā ñāṇaɱ tassa na vijjati."|| ||

988. "Bhotī carahi jānāti taɱ me akkhāhi pucchitā,||
Muddhaɱ muddhādhipātañ ca, taɱ suṇoma vaco tava."|| ||

989. "Ahaɱ p'etaɱ na jānāmi, ñāṇaɱ ettha na vijjati,||
Muddhaɱ muddhādhipāto cā Jinānaɱ h'eta dassanaɱ."|| ||

990. "Atha kho carahi jānāti asmiɱ puthuvimaṇḍale,||
Muddhaɱ muddhādhipātañ ca, taɱ me akkhāhi devate."|| ||

[192] 991. "Purā Kapilavatthumhā nikkhanto lokanāyako,||
Apacco Okkākarājassa Sakya-putto pabhaŋkaro.|| ||

992. So hi brāhmaṇa SamBuddho sabba-dhammāna pāragu,||
Sabbābhiññābalappatto sabba-dhammesu cakkhumā.||
Sabbadhammakkhayaɱ patto vimutto upadhi-sankhaye.|| ||

993. Buddho so Bhagavā loke dhammaɱ deseti cakkhumā,||
Taɱ tvaɱ gantvāna pucchassu so te taɱ vyākarissati."|| ||

994. 'SamBuddho' ti vaco sutvā udaggo Bāvarī ahu,||
Sok'assa tanuko āsi, pītiñ ca vipulaɱ labhi.|| ||

995. So Bāvarī atta-mano udaggo||
Taɱ devataɱ pucchati vedajāto,||
"katamambhi gāme nigamamhi vā pana||
katamamhi vā jana-pade lokanātho||
yattha gantvā namassemu sambuddhaɱ dipaduttamaɱ."|| ||

996. "Sāvatthiyaɱ Kosalamandire Jino||
Pahutapañño varabhūrimedhaso,||
So Sakya-putto vidhuro anāsavo||
Muddhādhipātassa vidu narāsabho.|| ||

997. Tato āmantayī sisse brāhmaṇe mattapārage,||
"Etha māṇavā akkhissaɱ suṇātha vacanaɱ mama.|| ||

[193] 998. Yass'eso dullabho loke pātu-bhāvo abhiṇhaso,||
Sv-ājja lokamhi uppanto SamBuddho iti vissuto||
Khippaɱ gantvāna Sāvatthiyaɱ passavho dipaduttamaɱ."|| ||

999. "Kathaɱ carahi jānemu disvā 'Buddho' ti brāhmaṇaɱ,||
Ajānataɱ no pabrūhi, yathā jānemu taɱ mayaɱ."|| ||

1000. "Āgatāni hi mantesu mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇā,||
Dvattiɱsā ca vyākhyātā samantā anupubbaso.|| ||

1001. Yass'ete honti gattesu mahā-purisa-lakkhaṇā,||
Dve va tassa gatiyo, tatiyā hi na vijjati.|| ||

1002. Sace agāraɱ ajjhāvasati, vijeyya paṭhaviɱ imaɱ,||
Adaṇḍena asatthena dhammena-m-anusāsāti.|| ||

1003. Sace ca so pabbajati agārā anagāriyaɱ,||
Vivattacchadedā SamBuddho arahā bhavati anuttaro.|| ||

1004. Jātiɱ gottañ ca lakkhaṇaɱ mante sisse punāpare,||
Muddhaɱ muddhādhipātañ ca manasā yeva pucchatha.|| ||

1005. Anāvaraṇadassāvi yadi Buddho bhavissati,||
Manasā pucchite pañhe vācāya vissajessati."|| ||

1006. Bāvarissa vaco sutvā sissā soḷasa brāhmaṇā,||
Ajito Tissa Metteyyo Puṇṇako atha Mettagu.|| ||

[194] 1007. Dhotako Upasivo ca Nando ca atha Hemako,||
Todeyya-Kappā dubhayo Jatukaṇṇi ca paṇḍito|| ||

1008. Bhaddāvudho Udayo ca Posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo,||
Mogharājā ca medhāvi Piŋgiyo ca mahā isi.|| ||

1009. Paccekagaṇino sabbe sabba-lokassa vissutā,||
Jhāyī jhāna-ratā dhīrā pubbavāsanavāsitā.|| ||

1010. Bāvariɱ abhivādetvā katvā ca naɱ padakkhiṇaɱ,||
Jaṭājinadharā sabbe pakkāmuɱ uttarāmukhā.|| ||

1011`. Aḷakassa Patiṭṭhānaɱ purimaɱ Māhissatiɱ tadā,||
Ujjeniñ cāpi Gonaddhaɱ Vedisaɱ Vanasavhayaɱ.|| ||

1012. Kosambīyaɱ cāpi Sāketaɱ Sāvatthiñ ca puruttamaɱ,||
Setavyaɱ Kapilavatthuɱ Kusinārañ ca mandiraɱ.|| ||

1013. Pāvañ ca Bhoganagaraɱ Vesāliɱ Māgadhaɱ puraɱ,||
Pāsāṇakaɱ cetiyañ ca ramaṇiyaɱ manoramaɱ.|| ||

[195] 1014. Tasito v'udakaɱ sītaɱ mahālābhaɱva vāṇijo,||
Chāyaɱ ghamm-ā-bhitatto va turitā pabbatam āruhuɱ.|| ||

1015. Bhagavā ca tamhi samaye bhikkhu-Saŋghapurakkhato,||
Bhikkhunaɱ dhammaɱ deseti, siho va nadati vane.|| ||

1016. Ajito addasa sambuddhaɱ vītaraɱsi va bhānumaɱ,||
Candaɱ yathā pannarase paripuriɱ upāgataɱ.|| ||

1017. Ath'assa gatte disvāna paripurañ ca vyañajanaɱ,||
eka-m-antaɱ ṭhito haṭṭho manopañhe apucchatha.|| ||

1018. "Ādissa jammanaɱ brūhi, gottaɱ brūhi salakkhaṇaɱ,||
Mantesu pāramiɱ brūhi, kati vāceti brāhmaṇo."|| ||

1019. "Visaɱvassa-sataɱ āyu so ca gottena Bāvari,||
Tiṇ'assa lakkhaṇā gatte, tiṇṇaɱ vedāna pāragu.|| ||

1020. Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe,||
Pañca satāni vāceti, sadhamme pāramiɱ gato."|| ||

[196] 1021. "Lakkhaṇānaɱ pavicayaɱ Bāvarissa naruttama,||
Taṇhacchida pakāsehi, mā no kaɱkhāyitaɱ ahu."|| ||

1022. "Mukhaɱ jivahāya chādeti, uṇṇ'assa bhamukantare,||
Kosohitaɱ vatthaguyhaɱ, evaɱ jānāhi māṇava."|| ||

1023. Pucchaɱ hi kiñci asuṇanto sutvā pañhe viyākate,||
Vicinteti jano sabbo vedajāto katañajali.|| ||

1024. 'Ko nu deve va Brahmā vā Indo vā pi Sujampati,||
Manasā pucchi te pañhe, kam etaɱ paṭibhāsati.'|| ||

1025. "Muddhaɱ muddhādhipātañ ca Bāvari paripucchati,||
Taɱ vyākarohi Bhagavā, kaŋkhaɱ vinaya no ise."|| ||

1026. "Avijjā muddhā ti jānāhi, vijjā muddhādhipātini,||
Saddhā satisamādhīhi chandaviriyena saɱyutā."|| ||

1027. Tato vedenana mahatā santhamahitvāna māṇavo,||
Ekaɱsaɱ ajinaɱ katvā pādesu sirasā pati.|| ||

1028. "Bāvari brāhmaṇo bhoto saha sissehi mārisa,||
Udaggacitto sumano pāde vandati cakkhuma."|| ||

[197] 1029. "Sukhito Bāvari hotu saha sissehi brāhmaṇo,||
Tvañ cāpi sukhino hohi ciraɱ jivāhi māṇava.|| ||

1030. Bāvarissa ca tuyahaɱ vā sabbesaɱ sabbasaɱsayaɱ,||
Katāvakāsā pucchavho yaɱ kiñci manas'icchatha."|| ||

1031. SamBuddhena katokāso nisīditvāna pañjali,||
Ajito paṭhamaɱ pañhaɱ tattha pucchi Tathāgataɱ|| ||

Vatthugāthā Niṭṭhitaɱ|| ||

 

 

2. Agitamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1032. Kena-ssu nivuto loko (icc-āyasmā Ajito) kena-ssu na-ppakāsati,||
Ki'ssābhilepanaɱ brūsi kiɱ su tassa mahabbhayaɱ."|| ||

1033. "Avijjāya nivuto loko (Ajitā ti Bhagavā)||
Vevicchā pamādā na-ppakāsati,||
Jappabhilepanaɱ brūmi dukkham assa mahabbhayaɱ.|| ||

[198] 1034. "Savanti sabbadhi sotā (icc-āyasmā Ajito)||
Sotānaɱ kiɱ nivāraṇaɱ||
Sotānaɱ saŋvaraɱ brūhi kena sotā pithiyare."|| ||

1035. "Yāni sotāni lokasmiɱ (Ajitā ti Bhagavā)||
Sati tesaɱ nivāraṇaɱ,||
Sotānaɱ saŋvaraɱ brūmi paññāy'ete pithiyyare."|| ||

1036. "Paññā c'eva sati ca (icc-āyasmā Ajito)||
Nāma-rūpañ ca mārisa,||
Etaɱ me puṭṭho pabrūhi katth'etaɱ uparujjhati."|| ||

1037. "Yam etaɱ pañhaɱ apucchi Ajita taɱ vadāmi te,||
Yattha nāmañ ca rūpañ ca asesaɱ uparujjhati,||
Viññāṇassa nirodhena etth'etaɱ uparujjhati."|| ||

1038. "Ye ca saŋkhāta-dhammāse ye ca sekhā puthu idha,||
Tesaɱ me nipako iriyaɱ puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisa."|| ||

1039. "Kāmesu nābhigijjheyya manasānāvilo siyā,||
Kusalo sabba-dhammānaɱ sato bhikkhu paribbaje" ti.|| ||

Agitamāṇava-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

 

3. Tissametteyyamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1040. "Ko'dhaɱ [199] saɱTusito loke (icc-āyasmā Tissa Metatayyo)||
Kassa no santi iñjitā,||
Ko ubh'anta-m-abhiññāya majjhe mantā na lippati,||
Kaɱ brūsi mahāpuriso ti ko idha sibbanīm accagā?"|| ||

1041. "Kāmesu Brahma-cariyavā (Metteyyā ti Bhagavā)||
Vitataṇho sadā sato,||
Saŋkhāya nibbuto bhikkhu||
Tassa no santi iñjitā.|| ||

1042. So ubh'anta-m-abhiññāya majjhe mantā na lippati,||
Taɱ brūmi mahāpuriso ti so idha sibbanim accagā" ti.|| ||

Tissametteyya-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

4. Puṇṇakamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1043. "Anejaɱ mula dassāviɱ (icc-āyasmā Puṇṇako)||
Atthi pañehana āgamaɱ||
[200] Kiɱ nissitā isayo manujā khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaɱ||
Yaññam akappayiɱsu puthu idha loke pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ."|| ||

1044. "Ye kec'ime isayo manujā (Puṇṇakā ti Bhagavā)||
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaɱ||
Yaññam akappayiɱsu puthu idha loke,||
Āsiɱmānā Puṇṇaka itthabhāvaɱ||
Jaraɱ sitā yaññam akappayiɱsu."|| ||

1045. "Ye kec'ime isayo manujā (icc-āyasmā Puṇṇako)||
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaɱ||
Yaññam akappayiɱsu puthu idha loke||
Kacciɱ su te Bhagavā yaññapathe appamattā||
Ātāru jātiñ ca jaraɱ ca mārisa||
Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ."|| ||

1046. "Āsiɱsanti thomayanti abhijappanti juhanti (Puṇṇakā ti Bhagavā)||
Kāmābhijappanti paṭicca lābhaɱ,||
Te yājayogā bhava-rāga-rattā||
Nātariɱsu jātijaran ti brūmi."|| ||

[201] 1047. "Te ce nātariɱsu yājayogā (icc-āyasmā Puṇṇako)||
Yaññehi jātiñ ca jarañ ca mārisa,||
Atha ko carahi deva-manussa-loke||
Atāri jātiñ ca jarañ ca mārisa||
Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ.|| ||

1048. "Saŋkhāya lokasmiɱ parovarāni (Puṇṇakā ti Bhagavā)||
Yass'iñjitaɱ n'atthi kuhiñci loke,||
Santo vidumo anigho nirāso||
Atāri so jātijaran ti brūmi" ti.|| ||

Puṇṇaka-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

5. Mettagūmāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1049. "Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ (icc-āyasmā Mettagu)||
Maññāmi taɱ vedaguɱ bhāvitattaɱ,||
Kuto nu dukkhā samudāgatā ime||
Ye keci lokasmiɱ anekarūpā."|| ||

[202] 1050. "Dukkhassa ve maɱ pabhavaɱ apucchasi (Mettagu ti Bhagavā)||
Taɱ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaɱ,||
Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā||
Ye keci lokasmiɱ anekarūpā.|| ||

1051. Yo ve avidvā upadhiɱ karoti||
Punappunaɱ dukkham upeti mando,||
Tasmā hi jānaɱ upadhiɱ na kayirā||
Dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassi."|| ||

1052. "Yan taɱ apucchimha akittayī no (icc-āyasmā Mettagu)||
Aññaɱ taɱ pucchāmi tad iŋgha brūhi||
Kathan nu dhīrā vitaranti oghaɱ||
Jātijaraɱ soka-pariddavañ ca,||
Taɱ me muni sādhu viyākarohi||
Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo."|| ||

1053. "Kittayissāmi te dhammaɱ (Mettagu ti Bhagavā) diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaɱ,||
yaɱ viditvā sato caraɱ tare loke visattikaɱ."|| ||

1054. "Tañ c'āhaɱ abhinandāmi mahesi dhammam uttamaɱ,||
Yaɱ viditvā sato caraɱ tare loke visattikaɱ."|| ||

1055. "Yaɱ kiñci sampajānāsi (Mettagu ti Bhagavā)||
Uddhaɱ adho tiriyaɱ cāpi majjhe,||
[203] Etesu nandiñ ca nivesanañ ca||
Panujja viññāṇaɱ bhave na tiṭṭhe.|| ||

1056. Evaɱ vihāri sato appamatto||
Bhikkhu caraɱ hitvā mamāyitāni,||
Jātijaraɱ soka-pariddavañ ca||
Idh'eva vidvā pajaheyya dukkhaɱ."|| ||

1057. "Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino, (icc-āyasmā Mettagu)||
Sukittitaɱ Gotama anupadhikaɱ,||
Addhā hi Bhagavā pahāsi dukkhaɱ||
Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo.|| ||

1058. Te cāpi nūna pajaheyyu dukkhaɱ||
Ye tvaɱ muni aṭṭhitaɱ ovadeyya,||
Taɱ taɱ namassāmi samecca nāga||
App-eva maɱ Bhagavā aṭṭhitaɱ ovadeyya."|| ||

1059. "Yaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ vedaguɱ ābhijaññā (Mettagu ti Bhagavā)||
Akiñcanaɱ kāma-bhave asattaɱ,||
Addhā hi so ogham imaɱ atāri||
Tiṇṇo ca pāraɱ akhilo akaŋkho.|| ||

1060. Vidvā ca so vedagu naro idha||
Bhavābhave saŋgam imaɱ visajja,||
[204] So vitataṇho anigho nirāso||
Atāri so jātijaran ti brūmi"ti.|| ||

Mettagumāṇava-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

6. Dhotakamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1061. "Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ, (icc-āyasmā Dhotako)||
Vācābhikaŋkhāmi mahesi tuyhaɱ,||
Tava sutvāna nigghosaɱ||
Sikekhe Nibbānam attano."|| ||

1062. "Tena h'ātappaɱ karohi, (Dhotakā ti Bhagavā)||
Idh'eva nipako sato,||
Ito sutvāna nigghosaɱ||
Sikkhe Nibbānam antano."|| ||

1063. "Passām'ahaɱ deva-manussa loke (icc-āyasmā Dhotako)||
Akiñcanaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ iriyamānaɱ,||
Taɱ taɱ namassāmi samantacakkhu||
Pamuñca maɱ Sakka kathaɱ-kathāhi."|| ||

1064. "Nāhaɱ gamissāmi pamocanāya (Dhotakā ti Bhagavā)||
Kathaɱkathiɱ Dhotaka kañci loke,||
Dhammañ ca seṭṭhaɱ ājānamāno||
Evaɱ tuvaɱ ogham imaɱ taresi."|| ||

1065. "Anusāsa brahme karaṇāyamāno (icc-āyasmā Dhotakā)||
Viveka-dhammaɱ, yam ahaɱ vijaññaɱ,||
[205] Yath'āhaɱ ākāso va avyāpajjamāno||
Idh'eva santo asito careyyaɱ."|| ||

1066. "Kittayissāmi te sattiɱ (Dhotakā ti Bhagavā)||
Diṭṭhe dhamema anitihaɱ,||
Yaɱ viditvā sato caraɱ tare loke visattikaɱ."|| ||

1067. "Taɱ c'āhaɱ abhinandāmi (icc-āyasmā Dhotako)||
Mahesi sattim uttamaɱ,||
Yaɱ viditvā sato caraɱ tare loke visattikaɱ."|| ||

1068. "Yaɱ kiñci sampajānāsi (Dhotakā ti Bhagavā)||
Uddhaɱ adho tiriyaɱ cāpi majjhe:||
Etaɱ viditvā 'saŋgo' ti loke||
Bhavābhavāya mā kāsi taṇhan" ti.|| ||

Dhotaka-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

7. Upasīvamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1069. "Eko ahaɱ Sakka mahantam oghaɱ (icc-āyasmā Upasivo)||
Anissito no visahāmi tārituɱ,||
Ārammaṇaɱ brūhi samantacakkhu.||
Yaɱ nissito ogham imaɱ tareyya".|| ||

1070. "Ākiñcaññaɱ pekkhamāno satimā (Upasivā ti Bhagavā)||
'N'atthī' ti nissāya tarassu oghaɱ,||
[206] Kāme pahāya virato kathāhi||
Taṇhakkhayaɱ nattamahābhipassa."|| ||

1071. "Sabbesu kāmesu yo vitarāgo (icc-āyasmā Upasivo)||
Ākiñcaññaɱ nissito hitvā-m-aññaɱ||
Saññā vimokkha parame vimutto,||
Tiṭṭhe nu so tattha anānuyāyī."|| ||

1072. "Sabbesu kāmesu yo vitarāgo (Upasivā ti Bhagavā )||
Ākiñcaññaɱ nissito hitvā-m-aññaɱ||
Saññā vimokkha parame vimutto,||
Tiṭṭheyya so tattha anānuyāyī."|| ||

1073. "Tiṭṭhe ce so tattha anānuyāyī (icc-āyasmā Upasivo)||
Yugam pi vassānaɱ samantacakkhu,||
Tatth'eva so sitisiyā vimutto||
bhavetha viññāṇaɱ tathāvidhassa."|| ||

1074. "Accī yathā vātavegena khitto (Upasīvā ti Bhagavā)||
atthaɱ paleti na upeti saɱkhaɱ, [207] Evaɱ muni nāmakāyā vimutto||
Anthaɱ paleti na upeti saŋkhaɱ."|| ||

1075. "Atthaɱ gato so uda vā so n'atthi (icc-āyasmā Upasivo)||
Udāhu ve sassatiyā arogo,||
Taɱ me muni sādu viyākarohi,||
Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo."|| ||

1076. "Atthaŋgatassa na pamāṇam atthi (Upasivā ti Bhagavā)||
Yena naɱ vajju, taɱ tassa n'atthi,||
Sabbesu dhammesu samuhatesu||
Samuhatā vādapathā pi sabbe" ti.|| ||

Upasiva-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

8. Nandamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1077. "'Santi loke munayo (icc-āyasmā Nando)||
Janā vadanti, ta-y-idaɱ kathaɱ su'||
Ñāṇupapannaɱ no muniɱ vadanti||
Udāhu ve jivitenūpapannaɱ."|| ||

1078. "Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena (Nandāni Bhagavā)||
Munidha Nanda kusalā vadanti,||
[208] Visenikatvā anighā nirāsā||
Caranti ye, te munayo ti brūmi."|| ||

1079. "Ye kec'ime samaṇa-brāhmaṇāse (icc-āyasmā Nando)||
Diṭṭhe sutenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ,||
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ||
Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiɱ||
Kaccis su te Bhagavā tattha yathā carantā||
Atāru jātiñ ca jarañ ca mārisa||
Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā, brūhi me taɱ."|| ||

1080. "Ye kec'ime samaṇa-brāhmaṇāse (Nandā ti Bhagavā)||
Diṭṭhe sutenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ,||
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ||
Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiɱ||
Kiñ cāpi te tattha yathā caranti,||
Nātariɱsu jātijaran ti brūmi."|| ||

1081. "Ye kec'ime samaṇa-brāhmaṇāse (icc-āyasmā Nando)||
Diṭṭhena sutenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ,||
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiɱ||
Anekarūpena vadanti suddhiɱ||
Sace muni brūsi anoghatiṇṇe||
[209] Atha ko carahi deva-manussa-loke,||
Atāri jātiñ ca jarañ ca mārisa,||
Pucchāmi taɱ Bhagavā, brūhi me taɱ."|| ||

1082. "Nāhaɱ'sabbe samaṇa-brāhmaṇāse (Nandā ti Bhagavā)||
Jātijarāya nivutā' ti brūmi||
Ye s'idha diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā||
Sīlabbataɱ vā pi pahāya sabbaɱ||
Anekarūpam pi pahāya sabbaɱ,||
Taṇhaɱ pariññāya anāsavāse,||
Te ve'narā oghatiṇṇā' ti brūmi."|| ||

1083. "Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino (icc-āyasmā Nando)||
Sukittitaɱ Gotama'anupadhikaɱ||
Ye s'idha diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ mutaɱ vā||
Sīlabbataɱ vā pi pahāya sabbaɱ||
Anekarūpam pi pahāya sabbaɱ,||
Taṇhaɱ pariññāya anāsavāse,||
Aham pi te 'oghatiṇṇā' ti brūmī' ti.|| ||

Nanda-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

9. Hemakamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1084. "Ye me pubbe viyākaɱsu (icc-āyasmā Hemako)||
[210] Huraɱ Gotama sāsanā,||
'Icc-āsi, iti bhavissati,'||
Sabbaɱ taɱ itihitihaɱ, sabbaɱ taɱ takkavaḍḍhanaɱ|| ||

1085. Nāhaɱ tattha abhiramiɱ.||
Tvañ ca me dhammam akkhāhi tañahā nigghātanaɱ muni,||
Yaɱ viditvā sato caraɱ tare loke visattikaɱ."|| ||

1086. "Idha diṭṭha suta viññātesu piyarūpesu Hemaka,||
Chandarāga vinodanaɱ nibbāṇa padam accutaɱ.|| ||

1087. Etad aññāya ye satā diṭṭhamadhamm-ā-bhinibbutā,||
Upasananā ca te sadā, — tiṇṇā loke visattikan" ti.|| ||

Hemaka-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

10. Todeyyamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1088. "Yasmiɱ kāmā na vasanti (icc-āyasmā Todeyyā)||
Taṇhā yassa na vijjati,||
Kathaɱkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, vimokho tassa kidiso.|| ||

[211] 1089. "Yasmiɱ kāmā na vasanti (Todeyyā ti Bhagavā)||
Taṇhā yassa na vijjati,||
Kathaɱkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, vimokho tassa nāparo."|| ||

1090. "Nirāsayo so uda āsasāno||
Paññāṇavā so uda paññakapapī,||
Muniɱ ahaɱ Sakka yathā vijaññaɱ||
Taɱ me viyācikkha samantacakkhu.|| ||

1091. "Nirāsayo so na so āsasāno||
Paññāṇavā so na ca paññakapapī,||
Evam pi Todeyya muniɱ vijāna||
Akiñcanaɱ kāma-bhave asattan" ti.|| ||

Todeyya-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

11. Kappamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1092. "Majjhe sarasmiɱ tiṭṭhataɱ (icc-āyasmā Kappo)||
Oghe jāte mahabbhaye,||
Jarāmaccuparetānaɱ dipaɱ pabrūhi mārisa;||
Tvañ ca me dipam akkhāhi, yathā-y-idaɱ nāparaɱ siyā."|| ||

[212] 1093. "Majjhe sarasmiɱ tiṭṭhataɱ (Kappā ti Bhagavā)||
Oghe jāte mahabbhaye,||
Jarāmaccuparetānaɱ dipaɱ pabrūmi kappa te|| ||

1094. Akiñcanaɱ anādānaɱ etaɱ dipaɱ anāparaɱ,||
Nibbānam iti naɱ brūmi, jarāmaccuparikkhayaɱ.|| ||

1095. Etad aññāya ye satā diṭṭha-dhamm-ā-bhinibbutā,||
Na te Māra-vasānugā, na te Mārassa paddhagu" ti.|| ||

Kappa-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

12. Gatukaṇṇimāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1096. "Sutvān'ahaɱ viraɱ akāmakāmiɱ (icc-āyasmā Jatukaṇṇi)||
Oghātigaɱ puṭṭhum akāmam āgamaɱ,||
Santipadaɱ brūhi sahajanetta,||
Yathātacchaɱ Bhagavā brūhi me taɱ.|| ||

1097. Bhagavā hi kāme Abhibhuyya iriyati||
Ādicco va paṭhaviɱ teji tejasā,||
Parittapaññassa me bhuripañña,||
Ācikkha dhammaɱ, yam ahaɱ vijaññaɱ||
Jātijarāya idha vippahānaɱ."|| ||

[213] 1098. "Kāmesu vinaya gedhaɱ (Jatukaṇṇi ti Bhagavā)||
Nekkhammaɱ daṭṭhu khemato,||
Uggahitaɱ nirattaɱ vā mā te vijjittha kiñcanaɱ.|| ||

1099. Yaɱ pubbe taɱ visosehi, pacchā te māhu kiñcanaɱ,||
Majjhe ce no gahessasi, upasanto carissasi.|| ||

1100. Sabbaso nāma-rūpasmiɱ vitagedhassa brāhmaṇa,||
Āsavāssa na vijjanti, yehi maccuvasaɱ vaje" ti.|| ||

Jatukaṇṇi-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

13. Bhadrāvudhamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1101. Okaɱjahaɱ taṇhacch'idaɱ anejaɱ (icc-āyasmā Bhadrāvudho)||
Nandiɱ jahaɱ oghatiṇṇaɱ vimuttaɱ,||
Kappaɱ jahaɱ abhiyāce sumedhaɱ||
Sutvāna nāgassa apanamissanti ito.|| ||

1102. Nānā janā jana-padehi saŋgatā||
Tava vīra vākyaɱ abhikaŋkhamānā,||
Tesaɱ tuvaɱ sādhu viyākarohi,||
Tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo."|| ||

1103. "Ādānataṇhaɱ vinayetha sabbaɱ (Bhadrāvudhā ti Bhagavā)||
Uddhaɱ adho tiriyañ cāpi majjhe,||
[214] Yaɱ yaɱ hi lokasmiɱ upādiyanti||
Ten'eva Māro anveti janatuɱ.|| ||

1104. Tasmā pajānaɱ na upādiyetha||
Bhikkhu sato kiñcanaɱ sabba-loke,||
'Ādānasatte' iti pekkhamāno||
Pajaɱ imaɱ maccudheyye visattan" ti.|| ||

Bhadrāvudha-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

14. Udayamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1105. "Jhāyiɱ virajam āsinaɱ (icc-āyasmā Udayo)||
Katakiccaɱ anāsavaɱ||
Pāraguɱ sabba-dhammānaɱ atthi pañehana āgamaɱ,||
Aññāvimokkhaɱ pabrūhi avijjāya pabhedanaɱ."|| ||

1106. "Pahānaɱ kāma-c-chandanaɱ (Udayā ti Bhagavā)||
Domanassānaɱ cūbhayaɱ,||
Thinassa ca panudanaɱ kukkuccānaɱ nivāraṇaɱ.|| ||

1107. Upekhā sati saɱsuddhaɱ dhammatakkapurejavaɱ,||
Aññāvimokkhaɱ pabrūmi avijjāya pabhedanaɱ."|| ||

[215] 1108. "Kiɱ su saŋyojano loko (icc-āyasmā Udayo)||
Kiɱ su tassa vicāraṇā,||
Kiss'assa vippahānena Nibbānam iti vuccati."|| ||

1109. "Nandi saŋyojano loko, (Udayā ti Bhagavā)||
Vitakkassa vicāraṇā,||
Taṇhāya vippabhānena Nibbānaɱ iti vuccati."|| ||

1110. "Kathaɱ satassa carato (icc-āyasmā Udayaɱ)||
Viññāṇaɱ uparujjhati,||
Bhagavantaɱ puṭṭhum āgamma taɱ suṇoma vaco tava."|| ||

1111. "Ajjhattañ ca bahiddhā ca vedanaɱ nābhinandito,||
Evaɱ satassa carato viññāṇaɱ uparujjhati" ti.|| ||

Udaya-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

15. Posālamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1112. "Yo atitaɱ ādisati (icc'āyasmā Posālo)||
Anejo chinnasaɱsayo,||
Pāraguɱ sabba-dhammānaɱ atthi pañhana āgamaɱ.|| ||

1113. Vibhūtarūpa-saññissa sabba-kāyappabhāyino||
Ajjhattañ ca bahiddhā ca 'n'atthi kiñci' ti passato,||
Ñāṇaɱ Sakkānu pucchāmi, kathaɱ neyyo tathā vidho."|| ||

[216] 1114. Viññāṇaṭṭhitiyo sabbā (Posolā ti Bhagavā)||
Abhijānaɱ Tathāgato||
Tiṭṭhantam enaɱ jānāti vimuttaɱ tapparāyaṇaɱ.|| ||

1115. Ākiñcaññā sambhavaɱ ñatvā 'nandi saŋyojanaɱ' iti,||
Evam evaɱ abhiññāya tato tattha vipassati:||
Etaɱ ñāṇaɱ tathaɱ tassa brāhmaṇassa vusimato" ti.|| ||

Posāla-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

16. Mogharāgamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus][than]

 

1116. "Dvāhaɱ Sakkaɱ apucchissaɱ (icc'āyasmā Mogharājā)||
Na me vyākāsi cakkhumā,||
'Yāva tatiyañ ca devisi vyākaroti' ti me sutaɱ.|| ||

1117. 'Ayaɱ loko, paro loko, Brahmaloko sa-devako,'||
Diṭṭhin te nābhijānāmi Gotamassa yasassino.|| ||

[217] 1118. Evaɱ abhikkantadassāviɱ atthi pañehana āgamaɱ,||
Kathaɱ lokaɱ avekkhantaɱ maccurājā na passati."|| ||

1119. "Suññato lokaɱ avekkhassu Mogharāja sadā sato,||
Attānudiṭṭhiɱ ūhacca, evaɱ maccutaro siyā;||
Evaɱ lokaɱ avekkhantaɱ maccurājā na passati" ti.|| ||

Mogharāja-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

17. Piŋgiyamāṇava-Pukkhā

[faus] [than]

 

1120. "Jiṇṇo'ham asmi abalo vitavaṇṇo (icc'āyasmā Piŋgiyo)||
Nettā na suddhā, savanaɱ na phāsu,||
Māhaɱ nassaɱ momuho antarāya||
Ācikkha dhammaɱ, yam ahaɱ vijaññaɱ||
Jātijarāya idha vippahānaɱ."|| ||

1121. "Disvāna rūpesu vihaññamāne (Piŋgiyā ti Bhagavā)||
Rūppanti rūpesu janā pamattā,||
Tasmā tuvaɱ Piŋgiya appamatto||
Jahassu rūpaɱ apuna-b-bhavāya."|| ||

1122. "Disā catasso vidisā catasso||
Uddhaɱ adho dasa disatā imāyo,||
[218] Na tuyhaɱ adiṭṭhaɱ asutaɱ-mutaɱ vā,||
Atho aviññāṇaɱ kiñcanam atthi loke||
Ācikkha dhammaɱ yam ahaɱ vijaññaɱ||
Jāti jarāya idha vippahānaɱ."|| ||

1123. "Taṇhādhipanne manuje pekkhamāno (Piŋgiyā ti Bhagavā)||
Santā pajā te jarasā parete,||
Tasmā tuvaɱ Piŋgiya appamatto||
Jahassu taṇhaɱ apuna-b-bhavāyā" ti.|| ||

Piŋgiya-Pukkhā Niṭṭhitā|| ||

 

 

Idam avoca Bhagavā Magadhesu viharanto Pāsāṇake cetiye, paricārikasoḷasānaɱ brāhmaṇānaɱ ajjhiṭṭho puṭṭho puṭṭho pañhe vyākāsi. Ekamekassa ce pi pañhassa attham aññāya dhammam aññāya dhamm-ā-nudhammaɱ paṭipajjeyya, gaccheyy'eva jarā-maraṇassa pāraɱ, pāraŋgamaniyā ime dhamma ti. Tasmā imassa dhamma-pariyāyassa Pārāyanan t'eva adhi vacanaɱ:|| ||

1124. Ajito Tissa-Metteyyo Puṇṇako atha Mettagu,||
Dhotako Upasivo ca Nando ca atha Hemako|| ||

[219] 1125. Todeyya-Kkappā dubhayo Jatukaṇṇi ca paṇiḍito,||
Bhadrāvudho Udayo ca Posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo,||
Mogharājā ca mekhāvi Piŋgiyo ca mahā isi.|| ||

1126. Ete Buddhaɱ upāgacchuɱ sampanna caraṇaɱ isiɱ||
Pucchantā nipuṇe pañeha Buddhaseṭṭhaɱ upāgamuɱ.|| ||

1127. Tesaɱ Buddho vyākāsi pañeha puṭṭho yathātathaɱ,||
Pañahānaɱ veyyā-karaṇena tosesi brāhmaṇe muni.|| ||

1128. Te tositā cakkhu-matā Buddhen'Ādiccabandhunā,||
Brahma-cariyam acariɱsu varapaññassa santike.|| ||

1129. Ekamekassa pañahassa yathā Buddhena desitaɱ,||
Tathā yo paṭipajjeyya, gacche pāraɱ apārato.|| ||

1130. Apārā paraɱ gaccheyya bhāvetto Maggam uttamaɱ,||
Maggo so pāraɱgamanāya, tasmā Parāyanaɱ iti.|| ||

 

 

"1131. Parāyanam anugāyissaɱ (icc-āyasmā Piŋgiyo)||
Yathā addakkhi, tathā akkhāsi, vimalo bhurimedhaso,||
Nikkāmo nibbano nātho kissa hetu musā bhaṇe|| ||

[220] 1132. Pahina mala mohassa mānamakkhappahāyino,||
Handāhaɱ kittayissāmi giraɱ vaṇṇupasaɱhitaɱ|| ||

1133. Tamonudo Buddho samantacakkhu||
Lokantagū sabba-bhavātivatto,||
Anāsavo sabba-dukkhappahino||
Saccavahayo brahme upāsito me.|| ||

1134. Dijo yathā kubbanakaɱ pahāya||
Bahupphalaɱ kānanaɱ āvaseyya,||
Evaɱ p'ahaɱ appadasse pahāya||
Mahodadhiɱ haɱsa-r-iv'ajjhapatto|| ||

1135. Ye'me pubbe viyākaɱsu||
Huraɱ Gotamasāsanā,||
'Icc'āsi, iti bhavissati,'||
Sabban taɱ itihitihaɱ, sabban taɱ takkavaḍḍhanaɱ.|| ||

1136. Eko tamanud'āsino jātimā so pabhaɱkaro,||
Gotamo bhuripaññāṇo, Gotamo bhurimedhaso.|| ||

[221] 1137. Yo me dhammam adesesi sandiṭṭhikam akālikaɱ,||
Taṇhakkhayam anitikaɱ, yassa n'atthi upamā kvaci.|| ||

1138. "Kin nu tamhā vippavasasi muhuttam api Piŋgiya,||
Gotamo bhuripaññāṇo, Gotamo bhurimedhaso.|| ||

1139. Yo te dhammam adesesi sandhiṭṭhikam akālikaɱ,||
Taṇhakkhayam anītikaɱ yassa n'atthi upamā kavaci.|| ||

1140. "Nāhaɱ tamhā vippamasāmi muhuttam api brāhmaṇa,||
Gotamo bhuripaññāṇā Gotamo bhūrimedhasā.|| ||

1141. Yo me dhammam adesesi sandhiṭṭhikam akālikaɱ,||
Taṇhakkhayam anitikaɱ, yassa n'atthi upamā kvaci.|| ||

1142. Passāmi naɱ manasā cakkhunā va||
Rattiɱ divaɱ brāhmaṇa appamatto||
Nama-s-samāno vivasemi-rattiɱ||
Ten'eva maññāmi avippavāsaɱ.|| ||

1143. Saddhā ca piti ca mano sati ca||
Nāpenti me Gotamasāsanamhā,||
Yaɱ yaɱ disaɱ vajati bhuripañño,||
Sa tena ten'eva nato'ham asmi.|| ||

[222] 1144. Jiṇṇassa me dubbalathāmakassa||
Ten'eva kāyo na paleti tattha,||
Saŋkappayattāya vajāmi niccaɱ,||
Mano hi me brāhmaṇa tena yutto|| ||

1145. Paŋke sayāno pariphandamāno dipā dipaɱ upapalaviɱ,||
Ath'addasāsiɱ SamaBuddhaɱ oghatiṇṇam anāsavaɱ.|| ||

1146. "Yathā ahu Vakkali muttasaddho||
Bhadrāvudho Āḷavi-Gotamo ca,||
Evam eva tvam pi pamuñcasasu saddhaɱ||
Gamissasi tvaɱ Piŋgiya maccudheyyapāraɱ."|| ||

1147. "Esa bhiyyo pasidāmi sutvāna munino vaco:||
Vivattacchaddo SamBuddho akhilo paṭibhānavā.|| ||

1148. Adhideve abhiññāya sabbaɱ vedi parovaraɱ,||
Pañahān'annakāro Satthā kaŋkhinaɱ paṭijānataɱ.|| ||

[223] 1149. Asaɱhiraɱ asaŋkuppaɱ, yassa n'atthi upamā kavaci,||
Addhā gamissāmi, na m'ettha kaŋkhā evaɱ maɱ dhārehi adhimuttacittan" ti.|| ||

Pārāyanavaggo Niṭṭhito|| ||

Suttanipāto samatto.|| ||
